# POST_GA 06 - Stats Drift Hygiene

> **Branch**: `post-ga/POST_GA_06_stats_drift_hygiene`
> **Status**: implemented; adversarial review pending
> **Spec ancestor(s)**: `post-ga-backlog-spec-v1alpha1.md`, `stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md`, `audit-chain-prediction-extension-v1alpha1.md`
> **Issues**: #157, #162
> **Estimated change size**: medium; stats aggregation, alert dedup, numeric guards

---

## §0. TL;DR

Add durable prediction drift alert dedup/cooldown and harden drift math
against NaN/Infinity so the stats aggregator emits stable, bounded
alerts.

## §1. Architectural Context

Stats aggregation converts audit prediction evidence into drift alerts.
The current GA path works, but post-GA issues call out alert dedup over
24 hours and numeric safety around invalid floating-point values.

## §2. Scope

- #157: 24h cooldown/dedup per `(tenant, model, agent_id, prompt_class)`
- #162: NaN/Infinity guard in drift alert math
- Tests for dedup, cooldown expiry, tenant isolation, and numeric guards
- Spec sync for alert source/event behavior only when runtime changes require it

## §3. Out of Scope

| Item | Pushed to |
|---|---|
| Drift event type doc cleanup | POST_GA_02 unless runtime changed |
| Dashboard/alert rule changes | Future observability slice unless required |
| Backfill of historical alerts | Not needed for forward hygiene |

## §4. File-Level Changes

- Modify `services/stats_aggregator/src/**`
- Add tests under stats aggregator test layout
- Add SQL migration only if dedup state needs durable storage
- Update `docs/stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md` if behavior changes
- Add evidence under `docs/reviews/post-ga/POST_GA_06_stats_drift_hygiene/`

## §5. Schema / Proto

Prefer an existing table or deterministic idempotency key if available.
Durable cooldown state lands in
`services/canonical_ingest/migrations/0022_prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns.sql`.
The primary key is exactly `(tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class)`;
`suppress_until` is indexed for expiry inspection. Key constraints mirror
the `canonical_events` aggregator mirror columns, including
character-count limits for multibyte-safe `agent_id` values and the same
7-class `prompt_class` enum. RLS is enabled and forced with a `FOR ALL`
policy using `app.current_tenant_id`; missing or invalid tenant context
fails closed. `last_z_score` rejects `NaN` and `+/-Infinity` at both
runtime and SQL CHECK layers. No proto changes.

## §6. Audit-Chain Impact

Dedup suppresses duplicate alert emission; it does not delete or mutate
prior audit rows. Suppressed decisions are observable through structured
logs and `spendguard_stats_aggregator_drift_alerts_suppressed_total`, so
operators can distinguish quiet cooldown from no drift.

## §7. Failure Modes

| Scenario | Expected behavior |
|---|---|
| Same drift repeats within 24h | Suppress duplicate alert |
| Same drift after cooldown | Emit once |
| Different tenant/model/agent/prompt | Independent cooldown key |
| Drift math produces NaN/Infinity | Fail closed; no audit payload or cooldown row is written |
| Dedup store unavailable before emit | Fail safe; do not spam immutable audit |
| Immutable append fails | No cooldown row is recorded; retry next cycle |
| Cooldown record fails after append | Alert remains durable; log duplicate-suppression risk |

## §8. Acceptance Gates

- `cargo build && cargo test` for `services/stats_aggregator`
- Dedup/cooldown tests cover same-key and different-key behavior
- Numeric tests cover NaN, Infinity, and division-by-zero cases
- Migration smoke if SQL added
- `make demo-up DEMO_MODE=default` if aggregator runtime path changes
- Evidence under `docs/reviews/post-ga/POST_GA_06_stats_drift_hygiene/`

Executed evidence is recorded in
`docs/reviews/post-ga/POST_GA_06_stats_drift_hygiene/verification.md`.

## §9. Review Checklist

1. Is the dedup key exactly `(tenant, model, agent_id, prompt_class)`?
2. Is the cooldown 24h and testable without sleeping?
3. Are NaN and Infinity impossible to emit into audit payloads?
4. Is tenant isolation preserved?
5. Does failure mode avoid alert spam?

## §10. Deferrals

| Item | Why deferred |
|---|---|
| Historical backfill | Not needed for forward alert hygiene |
| UI surfacing of suppressed alerts | Product UX |

## §11. Risk / Rollback

Risk is suppressing real alerts or spamming audit. Keep dedup key and
cooldown explicit, with metrics for suppression. Roll back by disabling
dedup only if alert spam risk is controlled by another gate.

## §12. AIT Execution Notes

Reviewer: codex CLI via `ait run --adapter codex --review adversarial`. Max 5 rounds. Staff+ panel arbitration if 5 rounds fail.

Reviewer should inspect dedup persistence and numeric edge tests.

## §13. Adoption History

| Role | Decision | Outcome |
|---|---|---|
| Software Architect | Keep stats hygiene separate from doc-only drift sync | POST_GA_06 vs POST_GA_02 |
| Backend Architect | Cooldown key must match issue text exactly | §7 |
| Security Engineer | Alert suppression must not hide tenant isolation issues | §9 |
| Database Optimizer | Durable dedup needs a bounded indexed key | §5 |
| Stats Domain Expert | NaN/Infinity are invalid alert payload values | §7 |
| Implementer self-review | PostgreSQL treats `NaN = NaN` as true, so the SQL CHECK must explicitly compare against `'NaN'::REAL` | Migration 0022 + `drift_alert_cooldown_postgres_rejects_non_finite_z_scores` |
| Staff+ panel | Store-unavailable behavior favors suppressing duplicates over immutable audit spam | §6/§7 |

## §14. Merge Checklist

- [x] #157 fixed and tested
- [x] #162 fixed and tested
- [x] Stats gates pass
- [ ] AIT review clean or Staff+ arbitration recorded
- [ ] Memory updated

## Test Coverage Added

- Postgres integration tests apply migration 0022 and verify same-key suppression, expiry, different-prompt allowance, different-tenant allowance, RLS, canonical 128-character multibyte `agent_id` acceptance, and SQL CHECK rejection for `NaN`, `Infinity`, and `-Infinity`.
- Numeric guard tests cover non-finite inputs, zero stddev, non-finite threshold, non-positive threshold at payload build, and non-finite alert payload rejection.

## Self-Review Notes

- PostgreSQL 16 returns true for `'NaN'::REAL = 'NaN'::REAL`; migration 0022 explicitly rejects `'NaN'::REAL` instead of relying on `x = x`.
- Round 2 reviewer found that pre-append cooldown reservation could turn append failures into 24h alert loss. Runtime now checks cooldown first and records cooldown only after durable append succeeds; failed append leaves the cooldown open for retry.
- Round 1 reviewer found that byte-length constraints could reject canonical multibyte `agent_id` values. Migration 0022 now mirrors canonical `char_length` constraints and enum constraints instead.

docs/reviews/post-ga/POST_GA_06_stats_drift_hygiene/round-1-fix.md
# Round 1 Fix

## Reviewer Finding

- P2: `prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns.agent_id` used `octet_length(agent_id) <= 256`, while canonical aggregator mirror columns allow `char_length(agent_id) <= 128`. A valid multibyte 128-character agent ID could be rejected by the cooldown store, causing fail-safe alert suppression.

## Fix

- Changed migration 0022 key constraints to mirror canonical aggregator columns:
  - `model`: `char_length(model) BETWEEN 1 AND 64`
  - `agent_id`: `char_length(agent_id) BETWEEN 1 AND 128`
  - `prompt_class`: canonical 7-class enum
- Updated tests to use canonical `rag` instead of non-canonical `rag_short`.
- Added `drift_alert_cooldown_postgres_accepts_canonical_multibyte_agent_id` with a 128-character CJK agent ID.

## Verification

- `cargo test --manifest-path services/stats_aggregator/Cargo.toml`: PASS

docs/reviews/post-ga/POST_GA_06_stats_drift_hygiene/round-2-fix.md
# Round 2 Fix

## Reviewer Findings

- Major: `detect_and_emit` wrote the 24h cooldown before signing and durable append. A transient signing or canonical_ingest failure could suppress a real alert for the full cooldown window even though no immutable alert existed.
- Minor: the non-finite z-score SQL test used synthetic `prompt_class` values that could also violate the prompt-class enum, making the test less isolated.

## Fix

- Split `DriftAlertCooldown` into `check` and `record_emitted`.
- `detect_and_emit` now checks cooldown before alert construction, signs and appends the CloudEvent, and records cooldown only after `sink.emit` succeeds.
- Failed append no longer writes cooldown; a follow-up cycle can retry the alert.
- If cooldown recording fails after a successful append, the durable alert is still counted and the daemon logs duplicate-suppression risk.
- The SQL CHECK test now binds legal `prompt_class = 'chat_short'` while varying only `last_z_score`.

## Verification

- `cargo fmt --manifest-path services/stats_aggregator/Cargo.toml`: PASS
- `cargo test --manifest-path services/stats_aggregator/Cargo.toml`: PASS
- `cargo build --manifest-path services/stats_aggregator/Cargo.toml`: PASS
- `helm template charts/spendguard --set chart.profile=demo`: PASS
- `helm template charts/spendguard -f charts/spendguard/values-production.example.yaml --set chart.profile=production`: PASS
- `make demo-down && make demo-up DEMO_MODE=default`: PASS
- `docker compose -f deploy/demo/compose.yaml up -d --build stats-aggregator && curl /healthz && curl /metrics`: PASS

# POST_GA_06 Round 3 Fixes

Reviewer: codex CLI direct adversarial fallback after AIT nested-wrapper failure.

## Findings Fixed

- Minor: numeric guard skips were not counted in
  `spendguard_stats_aggregator_drift_alerts_suppressed_total` even though the
  metric help text includes numeric safety guards.
- Minor: the Postgres cooldown key test covered tenant and prompt-class
  independence, but not model and agent-id independence.

## Implementation

- Added `numeric_guard_suppression_reason` in
  `services/stats_aggregator/src/drift_detector.rs`.
- `detect_and_emit` now increments `suppressed` and logs the reason when a
  non-finite value, non-positive baseline stddev, non-finite computed z-score,
  or invalid threshold suppresses alert emission.
- Expanded `drift_alert_cooldown_postgres_is_key_and_tenant_scoped` to verify
  independent cooldown behavior for all key dimensions:
  `(tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class)`.

     7	--
     8	-- This is mutable derived state owned by stats_aggregator. It gates
     9	-- prediction_drift_alert emission before a new immutable audit event is sent
    10	-- to canonical_ingest, so repeated drift in the same bucket does not spam the
    11	-- audit chain. It deliberately lives beside canonical_events because the

    27	        AND last_z_score <> 'Infinity'::REAL
    28	        AND last_z_score <> '-Infinity'::REAL
    29	    ),
    30	    updated_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT clock_timestamp(),
    31

    33	    CHECK (suppress_until > last_emitted_at)

   707	        agg.baseline_stddev = Some(20.0); // exclusive baseline
   708	                                          // z must be (150 - 100) / 20 = 2.5, NOT (150 - 140) / 100 = 0.1.

   850	    #[derive(Default)]
   851	    struct MemoryCooldown {
   852	        entries: parking_lot::Mutex<HashMap<DriftAlertKey, DateTime<Utc>>>,
   853	    }
   854	
   855	    #[async_trait::async_trait]
   856	    impl DriftAlertCooldown for MemoryCooldown {
   857	        async fn check(
   858	            &self,
   859	            key: &DriftAlertKey,
   860	            now: DateTime<Utc>,
   861	        ) -> Result<DriftAlertCooldownDecision, anyhow::Error> {
   862	            let entries = self.entries.lock();
   863	            if let Some(existing) = entries.get(key) {
   864	                if *existing > now {
   865	                    return Ok(DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Suppressed {
   866	                        suppress_until: *existing,
   867	                    });
   868	                }
   869	            }
   870	            let suppress_until = now + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS);
   871	            Ok(DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { suppress_until })
   872	        }
   873	
   874	        async fn record_emitted(
   875	            &self,
   876	            key: &DriftAlertKey,
   877	            emitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,
   878	            _z_score: f32,
   879	        ) -> Result<DateTime<Utc>, anyhow::Error> {
   880	            let suppress_until = emitted_at + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS);
   881	            let mut entries = self.entries.lock();
   882	            entries.insert(key.clone(), suppress_until);
   883	            Ok(suppress_until)
   884	        }
   885	    }

   260	fn numeric_guard_suppression_reason(
   261	    agg: &BucketAggregate,
   262	    cfg: &DriftDetectorConfig,
   263	) -> Option<&'static str> {
   264	    if !cfg.drift_z_threshold.is_finite() {
   265	        return Some("non-finite drift_z_threshold");
   266	    }
   267	    if cfg.drift_z_threshold <= 0.0 {
   268	        return Some("non-positive drift_z_threshold");
   269	    }
   270	
   271	    let Some(mean_7d) = agg.mean_7d else {
   272	        return None;
   273	    };
   274	    if !mean_7d.is_finite() {
   275	        return Some("non-finite mean_7d");
   276	    }
   277	
   278	    let Some(baseline_mean) = agg.baseline_mean else {
   279	        return None;
   280	    };
   281	    if !baseline_mean.is_finite() {
   282	        return Some("non-finite baseline_mean");
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    let Some(baseline_stddev) = agg.baseline_stddev else {
   286	        return None;
   287	    };
   288	    if !baseline_stddev.is_finite() {
   289	        return Some("non-finite baseline_stddev");
   290	    }
   291	    if baseline_stddev <= 0.0 {
   292	        return Some("non-positive baseline_stddev");
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    let z = (mean_7d - baseline_mean) / baseline_stddev;
   296	    (!z.is_finite()).then_some("non-finite z_score")
   297	}
   298	
   299	/// Build (but do not sign or emit) the prediction_drift_alert
   300	/// CloudEvent for a bucket. Separated from the emission step so unit
   301	/// tests can verify the envelope shape without a tonic Channel.
   302	pub fn build_drift_alert(
   303	    agg: &BucketAggregate,
   304	    z_score: f32,
   305	    cfg: &DriftDetectorConfig,
   306	) -> Option<CloudEvent> {
   307	    use bytes::Bytes;
   308	    if !drift_alert_payload_is_finite(agg, z_score, cfg) {
   309	        return None;
   310	    }
   311	    let now = Utc::now();
   312	    // R2 M2: payload reports baseline_* fields (window [now-30d, now-7d]
   313	    // — distinct from mean_30d which is the strategy-B cache baseline).
   314	    // Calibration-report consumers want both for trend analysis.
   315	    let data = serde_json::json!({
   316	        "tenant_id": agg.tenant_id.to_string(),
   317	        "model": agg.model,
   318	        "agent_id": agg.agent_id,
   319	        "prompt_class": agg.prompt_class,
   320	        "baseline_mean": agg.baseline_mean,
   321	        "baseline_stddev": agg.baseline_stddev,
   322	        "baseline_sample_size": agg.baseline_sample_size,
   323	        "current_mean_7d": agg.mean_7d,
   324	        "z_score": z_score,
   325	        "sample_size_7d": agg.sample_size_7d,
   326	        "sample_size_30d": agg.sample_size_30d,
   327	        "drift_z_threshold": cfg.drift_z_threshold,
   328	        "min_samples_for_alert": cfg.min_samples_for_alert,
   329	        "suggested_action": suggest_action(z_score),
   330	    });
   331	    let data_bytes = serde_json::to_vec(&data).unwrap_or_default();
   332	
   333	    Some(CloudEvent {
   334	        specversion: "1.0".to_string(),
   335	        r#type: PREDICTION_DRIFT_ALERT_EVENT_TYPE.to_string(),
   336	        source: format!("spendguard://stats-aggregator/{}", agg.tenant_id),
   337	        id: uuid::Uuid::now_v7().to_string(),
   338	        time: Some(prost_types::Timestamp {
   339	            seconds: now.timestamp(),
   340	            nanos: now.timestamp_subsec_nanos() as i32,
   341	        }),
   342	        datacontenttype: "application/json".to_string(),
   343	        data: data_bytes.into(),
   344	        tenant_id: agg.tenant_id.to_string(),
   345	        producer_signature: Bytes::new(),
   346	        ..Default::default()
   347	    })
   348	}
   349	
   350	fn drift_alert_payload_is_finite(
   351	    agg: &BucketAggregate,
   352	    z_score: f32,
   353	    cfg: &DriftDetectorConfig,
   354	) -> bool {
   355	    z_score.is_finite()
   356	        && cfg.drift_z_threshold.is_finite()
   357	        && cfg.drift_z_threshold > 0.0
   358	        && agg.baseline_mean.is_some_and(f32::is_finite)
   359	        && agg
   360	            .baseline_stddev
   361	            .is_some_and(|stddev| stddev.is_finite() && stddev > 0.0)
   362	        && agg.mean_7d.is_some_and(f32::is_finite)
   363	}

   365	/// Sink trait — abstracts the actual canonical_ingest gRPC call so
   366	/// tests can swap in an in-memory recorder.
   367	#[async_trait::async_trait]
   368	pub trait DriftAlertSink: Send + Sync {
   369	    async fn emit(&self, event: CloudEvent) -> Result<(), anyhow::Error>;
   370	}

   374	/// rejects this path when chart.profile=production.

   386	        Ok(())
   387	    }

   390	/// canonical_ingest sink emitting one AppendEventsRequest per alert.
   391	///
   392	/// R2 B5: AppendEventsRequest envelope MUST carry producer_id +
   393	/// schema_bundle + route or canonical_ingest's append handler rejects
   394	/// the call with `producer_id required` / `schema_bundle required` /
   395	/// `route is unspecified` (see
   396	/// services/canonical_ingest/src/handlers/append_events.rs:64,73,101).
   397	/// Defaults from R1 shape (`..Default::default()`) failed all three.
   398	pub struct CanonicalIngestDriftAlertSink {
   399	    client: tokio::sync::Mutex<CanonicalIngestClient<Channel>>,
   400	    producer_id: String,
   401	    schema_bundle_ref: SchemaBundleRef,
   402	    signing_key_id: String,
   403	}
   404	
   405	impl CanonicalIngestDriftAlertSink {
   406	    /// Build the sink with the envelope fields the canonical_ingest
   407	    /// handler requires.
   408	    ///
   409	    /// * `producer_id` — typically `stats-aggregator:<region>`; matches
   410	    ///   the `signer.producer_identity()` discipline used by tokenizer
   411	    ///   SLICE_05.
   412	    /// * `schema_bundle_ref` — pre-built SchemaBundleRef (id + hash +
   413	    ///   canonical_schema_version). Built in main.rs from config + the
   414	    ///   hex-decoded hash bytes (mirror of outbox_forwarder).
   415	    /// * `signing_key_id` — the AppendEventsRequest batch-level
   416	    ///   signing_key_id (transport check only; per-event signature is on
   417	    ///   each CloudEvent). Reuse signer.key_id() for consistency.
   418	    pub fn new(
   419	        channel: Channel,
   420	        producer_id: String,
   421	        schema_bundle_ref: SchemaBundleRef,
   422	        signing_key_id: String,
   423	    ) -> Self {
   424	        Self {
   425	            client: tokio::sync::Mutex::new(CanonicalIngestClient::new(channel)),
   426	            producer_id,
   427	            schema_bundle_ref,
   428	            signing_key_id,
   429	        }
   430	    }
   431	}
   432	
   433	#[async_trait::async_trait]
   434	impl DriftAlertSink for CanonicalIngestDriftAlertSink {
   435	    async fn emit(&self, event: CloudEvent) -> Result<(), anyhow::Error> {
   436	        let req = AppendEventsRequest {
   437	            producer_id: self.producer_id.clone(),
   438	            batch_max_producer_sequence: 0,
   439	            // batch_signature optional per Trace §13 — per-event
   440	            // signature on each CloudEvent is the canonical truth; we
   441	            // leave batch_signature empty (allowed in-cluster on mTLS).
   442	            batch_signature: bytes::Bytes::new(),
   443	            signing_key_id: self.signing_key_id.clone(),
   444	            schema_bundle: Some(self.schema_bundle_ref.clone()),
   445	            events: vec![event],
   446	            // OBSERVABILITY: drift_alert is an observability event, not
   447	            // an enforcement event. canonical_ingest's failure mode for
   448	            // OBSERVABILITY is buffer_then_retry (per Trace §10.1).
   449	            route: Route::Observability as i32,
   450	        };
   451	        let mut guard = self.client.lock().await;
   452	        let resp = guard
   453	            .append_events(req)
   454	            .await
   455	            .context("canonical_ingest AppendEvents")?;
   456	        ensure_append_accepted(resp.into_inner())
   457	    }
   458	}
   459	
   460	pub(crate) fn ensure_append_accepted(resp: AppendEventsResponse) -> Result<(), anyhow::Error> {
   461	    if resp.results.len() != 1 {
   462	        return Err(anyhow::anyhow!(
   463	            "AppendEvents prediction_drift_alert returned {} results for one event",
   464	            resp.results.len()
   465	        ));
   466	    }
   467	
   468	    let result = &resp.results[0];
   469	    let status = EventStatus::try_from(result.status).unwrap_or(EventStatus::Unspecified);
   470	    match status {
   471	        EventStatus::Appended | EventStatus::Deduped => Ok(()),
   472	        other => {
   473	            let error_message = result
   474	                .error
   475	                .as_ref()
   476	                .map(|err| err.message.as_str())
   477	                .filter(|msg| !msg.is_empty())
   478	                .unwrap_or("canonical_ingest returned no error detail");
   479	            warn!(
   480	                event_id = %result.event_id,
   481	                status = ?other,
   482	                err = %error_message,
   483	                "canonical_ingest rejected prediction_drift_alert"
   484	            );
   485	            Err(anyhow::anyhow!(
   486	                "AppendEvents prediction_drift_alert rejected event_id={} status={:?}: {}",
   487	                result.event_id,
   488	                other,
   489	                error_message
   490	            ))
   491	        }
   492	    }
   493	}
   494	
   495	/// Detect drift across a batch of bucket aggregates and emit signed
   496	/// CloudEvents for those exceeding the threshold. Returns the count of
   497	/// alerts emitted for metrics.
   498	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, Default, PartialEq, Eq)]
   499	pub struct DriftDetectionOutcome {
   500	    pub emitted: usize,
   501	    pub suppressed: usize,
   502	}
   503	
   504	pub async fn detect_and_emit(
   505	    aggregates: &[BucketAggregate],
   506	    cfg: &DriftDetectorConfig,
   507	    signer: &dyn Signer,
   508	    sink: &dyn DriftAlertSink,
   509	    cooldown: &dyn DriftAlertCooldown,
   510	) -> Result<DriftDetectionOutcome, anyhow::Error> {
   511	    let mut outcome = DriftDetectionOutcome::default();
   512	    for agg in aggregates {
   513	        if let Some(reason) = numeric_guard_suppression_reason(agg, cfg) {
   514	            outcome.suppressed += 1;
   515	            warn!(
   516	                tenant_id = %agg.tenant_id,
   517	                model = %agg.model,
   518	                agent_id = %agg.agent_id,
   519	                prompt_class = %agg.prompt_class,
   520	                reason,
   521	                "drift alert suppressed by numeric safety guard"
   522	            );
   523	            continue;
   524	        }
   525	        let z = match compute_z_score(agg) {
   526	            Some(z) => z,
   527	            None => continue,
   528	        };
   529	        let Some(n7d) = agg.sample_size_7d else {
   530	            continue;
   531	        };
   532	        if z.abs() <= cfg.drift_z_threshold || n7d < cfg.min_samples_for_alert {
   533	            continue;
   534	        }
   535	        let key = DriftAlertKey::from(agg);
   536	        match cooldown.check(&key, Utc::now()).await {
   537	            Ok(DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }) => {}
   538	            Ok(DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Suppressed { suppress_until }) => {
   539	                outcome.suppressed += 1;
   540	                info!(
   541	                    tenant_id = %agg.tenant_id,
   542	                    model = %agg.model,
   543	                    agent_id = %agg.agent_id,
   544	                    prompt_class = %agg.prompt_class,
   545	                    suppress_until = %suppress_until,
   546	                    "drift alert suppressed by cooldown"
   547	                );
   548	                continue;
   549	            }
   550	            Err(e) => {
   551	                outcome.suppressed += 1;
   552	                warn!(
   553	                    tenant_id = %agg.tenant_id,
   554	                    model = %agg.model,
   555	                    agent_id = %agg.agent_id,
   556	                    prompt_class = %agg.prompt_class,
   557	                    error = %e,
   558	                    "drift alert cooldown unavailable; suppressing alert to avoid immutable audit spam"
   559	                );
   560	                continue;

     1	//! Drift detection + signed CloudEvent emission per spec
     2	//! stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §7.
     3	//!
     4	//! ## Algorithm (spec §7.1)
     5	//!
     6	//! For each (tenant, model, agent_id, prompt_class) bucket whose 7d AND
     7	//! 30d windows both have data:
     8	//!
     9	//! ```text
    10	//! z_score = (mean_7d - mean_30d) / stddev_30d
    11	//!
    12	//! IF |z_score| > drift_z_threshold (default 2.0)
    13	//!    AND sample_size_7d >= MIN_SAMPLES_FOR_ALERT (default 100):
    14	//!   emit prediction_drift_alert CloudEvent
    15	//! ```
    16	//!
    17	//! The threshold is configurable per spec §0.3 GA prereq #1 ("per-tenant
    18	//! override"); SLICE_06 ships the global config; per-tenant override is
    19	//! SLICE-extra.
    20	//!
    21	//! ## Audit-routed CloudEvent
    22	//!
    23	//! Per SLICE_05 R2 B2 + tokenizer worker convention (worker.rs:72-81),
    24	//! drift_alert events use the `spendguard.audit.*` prefix to route into
    25	//! canonical_ingest's ImmutableAuditLog. The fallthrough
    26	//! `spendguard.prediction.*` (used in early drafts of the spec §7.2
    27	//! example YAML) would route to ProfilePayloadBlob which is
    28	//! RTBF-deletable and violates the spec §0.1 immutability claim.
    29	
    30	use anyhow::Context;
    31	use chrono::{DateTime, Duration as ChronoDuration, Utc};
    32	use prost::Message;
    33	use spendguard_signing::Signer;
    34	use sqlx::postgres::PgPool;
    35	use tonic::transport::Channel;
    36	use tracing::{debug, info, warn};
    37	
    38	use crate::aggregation::BucketAggregate;
    39	use crate::proto::canonical_ingest::v1::{
    40	    append_events_request::Route, canonical_ingest_client::CanonicalIngestClient,
    41	    event_result::Status as EventStatus, AppendEventsRequest, AppendEventsResponse,
    42	};
    43	use crate::proto::common::v1::{CloudEvent, SchemaBundleRef};
    44	
    45	/// CloudEvent type for prediction drift alerts. Per spec §7.2 family
    46	/// + SLICE_05 R2 B2 audit-routed prefix discipline.
    47	pub const PREDICTION_DRIFT_ALERT_EVENT_TYPE: &str =
    48	    "spendguard.audit.prediction_drift_alert.v1alpha1";
    49	
    50	/// Configuration shared from main.rs into the drift detector. Pulled out
    51	/// of the daemon config so the detector module is unit-testable without
    52	/// the full envy + sqlx + tonic stack.
    53	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
    54	pub struct DriftDetectorConfig {
    55	    pub drift_z_threshold: f32,
    56	    pub min_samples_for_alert: i32,
    57	}
    58	
    59	pub const DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS: i64 = 24;
    60	
    61	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
    62	pub struct DriftAlertKey {
    63	    pub tenant_id: uuid::Uuid,
    64	    pub model: String,
    65	    pub agent_id: String,
    66	    pub prompt_class: String,
    67	}
    68	
    69	impl From<&BucketAggregate> for DriftAlertKey {
    70	    fn from(agg: &BucketAggregate) -> Self {
    71	        Self {
    72	            tenant_id: agg.tenant_id,
    73	            model: agg.model.clone(),
    74	            agent_id: agg.agent_id.clone(),
    75	            prompt_class: agg.prompt_class.clone(),
    76	        }
    77	    }
    78	}
    79	
    80	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
    81	pub enum DriftAlertCooldownDecision {
    82	    Allowed { suppress_until: DateTime<Utc> },
    83	    Suppressed { suppress_until: DateTime<Utc> },
    84	}
    85	
    86	#[async_trait::async_trait]
    87	pub trait DriftAlertCooldown: Send + Sync {
    88	    async fn check(
    89	        &self,
    90	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
    91	        now: DateTime<Utc>,
    92	    ) -> Result<DriftAlertCooldownDecision, anyhow::Error>;
    93	
    94	    async fn record_emitted(
    95	        &self,
    96	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
    97	        emitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,
    98	        z_score: f32,
    99	    ) -> Result<DateTime<Utc>, anyhow::Error>;
   100	}
   101	
   102	pub struct PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore {
   103	    pool: PgPool,
   104	}
   105	
   106	impl PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore {
   107	    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {
   108	        Self { pool }
   109	    }
   110	}
   111	
   112	#[async_trait::async_trait]
   113	impl DriftAlertCooldown for PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore {
   114	    async fn check(
   115	        &self,
   116	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
   117	        now: DateTime<Utc>,
   118	    ) -> Result<DriftAlertCooldownDecision, anyhow::Error> {
   119	        let mut tx = self.pool.begin().await.context("begin drift cooldown tx")?;
   120	        sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   121	            .bind(key.tenant_id.to_string())
   122	            .execute(&mut *tx)
   123	            .await
   124	            .context("set RLS tenant_id for prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns")?;
   125	
   126	        let active_until = sqlx::query_scalar::<_, DateTime<Utc>>(
   127	            r#"
   128	            SELECT suppress_until
   129	            FROM prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns
   130	            WHERE tenant_id = $1
   131	              AND model = $2
   132	              AND agent_id = $3
   133	              AND prompt_class = $4
   134	            "#,
   135	        )
   136	        .bind(key.tenant_id)
   137	        .bind(&key.model)
   138	        .bind(&key.agent_id)
   139	        .bind(&key.prompt_class)
   140	        .fetch_optional(&mut *tx)
   141	        .await
   142	        .context("read prediction_drift_alert cooldown")?;
   143	
   144	        let decision = match active_until {
   145	            Some(until) if until > now => DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Suppressed {
   146	                suppress_until: until,
   147	            },
   148	            _ => DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed {
   149	                suppress_until: now + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS),
   150	            },
   151	        };
   152	
   153	        tx.commit()
   154	            .await
   155	            .context("commit drift cooldown check tx")?;
   156	        Ok(decision)
   157	    }
   158	
   159	    async fn record_emitted(
   160	        &self,
   161	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
   162	        emitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,
   163	        z_score: f32,
   164	    ) -> Result<DateTime<Utc>, anyhow::Error> {
   165	        if !z_score.is_finite() {
   166	            anyhow::bail!("non-finite z_score cannot enter drift alert cooldown store");
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        let suppress_until = emitted_at + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS);
   170	        let mut tx = self.pool.begin().await.context("begin drift cooldown tx")?;
   171	        sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   172	            .bind(key.tenant_id.to_string())
   173	            .execute(&mut *tx)
   174	            .await
   175	            .context("set RLS tenant_id for prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns")?;
   176	
   177	        let recorded_until = sqlx::query_scalar::<_, DateTime<Utc>>(
   178	            r#"
   179	            INSERT INTO prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns (
   180	              tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class,
   181	              last_emitted_at, suppress_until, last_z_score, updated_at
   182	            )
   183	            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, clock_timestamp())
   184	            ON CONFLICT (tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class)
   185	              DO UPDATE SET
   186	                last_emitted_at = EXCLUDED.last_emitted_at,
   187	                suppress_until = EXCLUDED.suppress_until,
   188	                last_z_score = EXCLUDED.last_z_score,
   189	                updated_at = clock_timestamp()
   190	            RETURNING suppress_until
   191	            "#,
   192	        )
   193	        .bind(key.tenant_id)
   194	        .bind(&key.model)
   195	        .bind(&key.agent_id)
   196	        .bind(&key.prompt_class)
   197	        .bind(emitted_at)
   198	        .bind(suppress_until)
   199	        .bind(z_score)
   200	        .fetch_one(&mut *tx)
   201	        .await
   202	        .context("record prediction_drift_alert cooldown")?;
   203	
   204	        tx.commit().await.context("commit drift cooldown tx")?;
   205	        Ok(recorded_until)
   206	    }
   207	}
   208	
   209	/// Per spec §7.3 suggested action heuristic.
   210	fn suggest_action(z_score: f32) -> &'static str {
   211	    if z_score > 0.0 {
   212	        "investigate_agent_change"
   213	    } else {
   214	        "review_predictor_baseline"
   215	    }
   216	}
   217	
   218	/// Compute z-score per spec §7.1.
   219	///
   220	/// R2 M2 (Software F5): baseline EXCLUDES the current 7-day window.
   221	/// R1 shape used mean_30d (which includes the last 7d) → baseline was
   222	/// contaminated by the very window we were comparing against, biasing
   223	/// z toward 0. Now we read baseline_mean / baseline_stddev which were
   224	/// computed over [now - 30d, now - 7d] (see aggregation.rs::agg_baseline).
   225	///
   226	/// Returns None when:
   227	///   * 7d window is missing (no current sample to compare)
   228	///   * baseline window is missing (new bucket; first activity in 7d)
   229	///   * baseline_stddev == 0 (all baseline samples identical → undefined ratio)
   230	pub fn compute_z_score(agg: &BucketAggregate) -> Option<f32> {
   231	    let mean_7d = agg.mean_7d?;
   232	    let baseline_mean = agg.baseline_mean?;
   233	    let baseline_stddev = agg.baseline_stddev?;
   234	    if !mean_7d.is_finite() || !baseline_mean.is_finite() || !baseline_stddev.is_finite() {
   235	        return None;
   236	    }
   237	    if baseline_stddev <= 0.0 {
   238	        // baseline_stddev == 0 → all baseline samples identical.
   239	        // Strict spec interpretation: z-score is undefined → no alert.
   240	        return None;
   241	    }
   242	    let z = (mean_7d - baseline_mean) / baseline_stddev;
   243	    z.is_finite().then_some(z)
   244	}
   245	
   246	/// Decision predicate: should this bucket emit a drift alert?
   247	pub fn should_emit_drift_alert(agg: &BucketAggregate, cfg: &DriftDetectorConfig) -> bool {
   248	    if !cfg.drift_z_threshold.is_finite() || cfg.drift_z_threshold <= 0.0 {
   249	        return false;
   250	    }
   251	    let Some(z) = compute_z_score(agg) else {
   252	        return false;
   253	    };
   254	    let Some(n7d) = agg.sample_size_7d else {
   255	        return false;
   256	    };
   257	    z.abs() > cfg.drift_z_threshold && n7d >= cfg.min_samples_for_alert
   258	}

     1	//! SpendGuard stats_aggregator daemon entry point.
     2	//!
     3	//! Spec ref stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §2.
     4	//!
     5	//! SLICE_06 boot sequence:
     6	//!
     7	//!   1. Install rustls aws_lc_rs crypto provider.
     8	//!   2. Load env config via [`spendguard_stats_aggregator::config::Config`].
     9	//!   3. Connect to canonical_ingest DB (read source + cache write target).
    10	//!   4. Connect to canonical_ingest gRPC for signed CloudEvent emission
    11	//!      (LoggingDriftAlertSink fallback when URL is empty — demo only;
    12	//!      production Helm gate enforces).
    13	//!   5. Spawn metrics hyper server (/metrics + /healthz + /readyz).
    14	//!   6. Run the scheduler loop (hourly per spec §8.1) until shutdown.
    15	//!
    16	//! Container security: USER 65532 + readOnlyRootFilesystem + cap_drop ALL
    17	//! enforced by the Helm chart (Phase F). The daemon itself has no
    18	//! privileged needs (no UDS bind, no socket bind besides the metrics TCP).
    19	
    20	use std::net::SocketAddr;
    21	use std::sync::Arc;
    22	use std::time::Duration;
    23	
    24	use anyhow::{Context, Result};
    25	use tonic::transport::{Certificate, ClientTlsConfig, Endpoint, Identity};
    26	use tracing::{error, info, warn};
    27	use tracing_subscriber::EnvFilter;
    28	
    29	use spendguard_signing::Signer;
    30	use spendguard_stats_aggregator::{
    31	    aggregation::STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
    32	    config::Config,
    33	    drift_detector::{
    34	        CanonicalIngestDriftAlertSink, DriftAlertCooldown, DriftAlertSink, DriftDetectorConfig,
    35	        LoggingDriftAlertSink, PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore,
    36	    },
    37	    scheduler::run_loop,
    38	};
    39	
    40	#[tokio::main]
    41	async fn main() -> Result<()> {
    42	    rustls::crypto::aws_lc_rs::default_provider()
    43	        .install_default()
    44	        .map_err(|_| anyhow::anyhow!("failed to install rustls aws_lc_rs default provider"))?;
    45	
    46	    init_tracing();
    47	
    48	    let cfg = Config::from_env().context("loading stats_aggregator config")?;
    49	    info!(
    50	        cycle_seconds = cfg.cycle_seconds,
    51	        min_samples_for_alert = cfg.min_samples_for_alert,
    52	        drift_z_threshold = cfg.drift_z_threshold,
    53	        metrics_addr = %cfg.metrics_addr,
    54	        region = %cfg.region,
    55	        profile = %cfg.profile,
    56	        canonical_ingest_url = %cfg.canonical_ingest_url,
    57	        database_present = !cfg.database_url.is_empty(),
    58	        advisory_lock_id = STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
    59	        "starting spendguard-stats-aggregator"
    60	    );
    61	
    62	    // ── Validate config gates ─────────────────────────────────────
    63	    if cfg.database_url.is_empty() {
    64	        anyhow::bail!(
    65	            "SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR_DATABASE_URL is required (canonical_ingest read+write source)"
    66	        );
    67	    }
    68	    if cfg.cycle_seconds < 60 {
    69	        warn!(
    70	            cycle_seconds = cfg.cycle_seconds,
    71	            "cycle_seconds < 60 — clamping to 60 to protect Postgres"
    72	        );
    73	    }
    74	    let cycle_seconds = cfg.cycle_seconds.max(60);
    75	
    76	    // ── Connect to canonical_ingest DB ────────────────────────────
    77	    let pool = sqlx::postgres::PgPoolOptions::new()
    78	        .max_connections(8)
    79	        .acquire_timeout(Duration::from_secs(10))
    80	        .connect(&cfg.database_url)
    81	        .await
    82	        .context("connect to canonical_ingest DB")?;
    83	    info!("canonical_ingest DB pool connected");
    84	
    85	    // ── Signer (audit-routed CloudEvent producer identity) ────────
    86	    //
    87	    // R2 M10: do NOT std::env::set_var() — that mutation is racy on
    88	    // multi-threaded Rust (Rust 1.80+ marks set_var unsafe in code
    89	    // running concurrently with other env reads). The signer crate's
    90	    // signer_from_env reads `<prefix>_SIGNING_PRODUCER_IDENTITY`
    91	    // directly; Helm sets this env var at pod startup (see
    92	    // charts/spendguard/templates/stats_aggregator.yaml). No runtime
    93	    // mutation required.
    94	    let signer: Arc<dyn Signer> = Arc::from(
    95	        spendguard_signing::signer_from_env("SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR")
    96	            .await
    97	            .context("load Ed25519 signer for prediction_drift_alert CloudEvent signing")?,
    98	    );
    99	    info!(
   100	        producer_identity = %signer.producer_identity(),
   101	        key_id = %signer.key_id(),
   102	        "signer ready"
   103	    );
   104	
   105	    // ── Build drift alert sink ────────────────────────────────────
   106	    //
   107	    // R2 B5: production sink construction requires schema_bundle_id +
   108	    // schema_bundle_hash_hex from config so the AppendEventsRequest
   109	    // envelope carries the required fields. Demo profile may use the
   110	    // LoggingDriftAlertSink which skips the envelope entirely.
   111	    let sink: Arc<dyn DriftAlertSink> = if cfg.canonical_ingest_url.is_empty() {
   112	        warn!(
   113	            "SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR_CANONICAL_INGEST_URL not set — \
   114	             drift_alert events will log to stdout (demo mode). \
   115	             Production Helm profile rejects this fallback."
   116	        );
   117	        Arc::new(LoggingDriftAlertSink)
   118	    } else {
   119	        if cfg.schema_bundle_id.is_empty() {
   120	            anyhow::bail!(
   121	                "SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR_SCHEMA_BUNDLE_ID required when \
   122	                 SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR_CANONICAL_INGEST_URL is set \
   123	                 (R2 B5: canonical_ingest rejects AppendEventsRequest \
   124	                 without schema_bundle)"
   125	            );
   126	        }
   127	        if cfg.schema_bundle_hash_hex.is_empty() {
   128	            anyhow::bail!(
   129	                "SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR_SCHEMA_BUNDLE_HASH_HEX required \
   130	                 when SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR_CANONICAL_INGEST_URL is set"
   131	            );
   132	        }
   133	        let bundle_hash = hex::decode(&cfg.schema_bundle_hash_hex)
   134	            .context("SPENDGUARD_STATS_AGGREGATOR_SCHEMA_BUNDLE_HASH_HEX must be hex-encoded")?;
   135	        let schema_bundle_ref = spendguard_stats_aggregator::proto::common::v1::SchemaBundleRef {
   136	            schema_bundle_id: cfg.schema_bundle_id.clone(),
   137	            schema_bundle_hash: bundle_hash.into(),
   138	            canonical_schema_version: cfg.canonical_schema_version.clone(),
   139	        };
   140	        let channel = build_canonical_ingest_channel(&cfg)
   141	            .await
   142	            .context("connect canonical_ingest channel")?;
   143	        info!(
   144	            url = %cfg.canonical_ingest_url,
   145	            mtls = cfg.sink_tls_cert_pem.is_some(),
   146	            schema_bundle_id = %cfg.schema_bundle_id,
   147	            "canonical_ingest sink connected"
   148	        );
   149	        Arc::new(CanonicalIngestDriftAlertSink::new(
   150	            channel,
   151	            signer.producer_identity().to_string(),
   152	            schema_bundle_ref,
   153	            signer.key_id().to_string(),
   154	        ))
   155	    };
   156	
   157	    let detector_cfg = DriftDetectorConfig {
   158	        drift_z_threshold: cfg.drift_z_threshold,
   159	        min_samples_for_alert: cfg.min_samples_for_alert,
   160	    };
   161	    let cooldown: Arc<dyn DriftAlertCooldown> =
   162	        Arc::new(PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore::new(pool.clone()));
   163	
   164	    // ── Spawn metrics server ──────────────────────────────────────
   165	    //
   166	    // R2 M8: pass the DB pool + cycle-staleness threshold so /healthz +
   167	    // /readyz can probe real subsystem state. /livez stays as pure
   168	    // process liveness ("ok"). /readyz fails if no cycle has run in
   169	    // 2× cycle_seconds (operator alert on stuck scheduler).
   170	    if !cfg.metrics_addr.is_empty() {
   171	        let addr: SocketAddr = cfg
   172	            .metrics_addr
   173	            .parse()
   174	            .with_context(|| format!("invalid metrics_addr `{}`", cfg.metrics_addr))?;
   175	        let pool_for_health = pool.clone();
   176	        let max_cycle_age_secs = cycle_seconds.saturating_mul(2);
   177	        tokio::spawn(async move {
   178	            if let Err(e) = run_metrics_server(addr, pool_for_health, max_cycle_age_secs).await {
   179	                error!(?e, "metrics server exited with error");
   180	            }
   181	        });
   182	        info!(
   183	            addr = %cfg.metrics_addr,
   184	            max_cycle_age_secs,
   185	            "metrics endpoint bound"
   186	        );
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    // ── Run scheduler loop (forever, until ctrl-c) ────────────────
   190	    let pool_for_loop = pool.clone();
   191	    let scheduler_handle = tokio::spawn(async move {
   192	        run_loop(
   193	            pool_for_loop,
   194	            cycle_seconds,
   195	            detector_cfg,
   196	            signer,
   197	            sink,
   198	            cooldown,
   199	        )
   200	        .await;
   201	    });
   202	
   203	    shutdown_signal().await;
   204	    scheduler_handle.abort();
   205	    info!("spendguard-stats-aggregator shut down cleanly");
   206	    Ok(())
   207	}

     1	//! Cycle scheduler per spec stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §8.
     2	//!
     3	//! ## Loop shape
     4	//!
     5	//! ```text
     6	//! loop {
     7	//!   sleep(cycle_seconds);
     8	//!   if try_acquire_lock() {
     9	//!     for tenant in discover_active_tenants():
    10	//!       aggregate_output_distribution(tenant)
    11	//!       aggregate_run_length(tenant)
    12	//!     detect_and_emit(aggregates)
    13	//!     release_lock()
    14	//!   } else {
    15	//!     metric: stats_aggregator_skipped_lock_held
    16	//!   }
    17	//! }
    18	//! ```
    19	//!
    20	//! Per spec §8.1 default cadence is hourly. Per-tenant cadence override
    21	//! (spec §8.2) is deferred to SLICE-extra; the scheduler currently
    22	//! treats every tenant uniformly.
    23	
    24	use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicU64, Ordering};
    25	use std::sync::Arc;
    26	use std::time::Duration;
    27	
    28	use anyhow::Context;
    29	use sqlx::postgres::PgPool;
    30	use tokio::time::interval;
    31	use tracing::{error, info, warn};
    32	
    33	use crate::aggregation::{
    34	    aggregate_output_distribution, discover_active_tenants, release_lock_conn,
    35	    try_acquire_lock_conn,
    36	};
    37	use crate::drift_detector::{
    38	    detect_and_emit, DriftAlertCooldown, DriftAlertSink, DriftDetectorConfig,
    39	};
    40	use crate::run_length::aggregate_run_length;
    41	use spendguard_signing::Signer;
    42	
    43	// R2 M13 (Software F15): real counters incremented from the cycle
    44	// loop. Rendered into the /metrics body. Exposed as `pub static` so
    45	// render_metrics in main.rs reads the live values without a global
    46	// registry.
    47	pub static CYCLES_TOTAL: AtomicU64 = AtomicU64::new(0);
    48	pub static SKIPPED_LOCK_HELD_TOTAL: AtomicU64 = AtomicU64::new(0);
    49	pub static DRIFT_ALERTS_TOTAL: AtomicU64 = AtomicU64::new(0);
    50	pub static DRIFT_ALERTS_SUPPRESSED_TOTAL: AtomicU64 = AtomicU64::new(0);
    51	pub static CYCLE_ERROR_TOTAL: AtomicU64 = AtomicU64::new(0);
    52	pub static LAST_CYCLE_START_UNIX_SECS: AtomicU64 = AtomicU64::new(0);
    53	
    54	/// One cycle's outcome surfaced for metric counters.
    55	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
    56	pub struct CycleOutcome {
    57	    pub lock_acquired: bool,
    58	    pub tenants_processed: usize,
    59	    pub alerts_emitted: usize,
    60	    pub alerts_suppressed: usize,
    61	    pub error_count: usize,
    62	}
    63	
    64	/// Run one full aggregation cycle. Exposed separately from the loop so
    65	/// integration tests can invoke a single cycle.
    66	pub async fn run_one_cycle(
    67	    pool: &PgPool,
    68	    cfg: &DriftDetectorConfig,
    69	    signer: Arc<dyn Signer>,
    70	    sink: Arc<dyn DriftAlertSink>,
    71	    cooldown: Arc<dyn DriftAlertCooldown>,
    72	) -> Result<CycleOutcome, anyhow::Error> {
    73	    let mut outcome = CycleOutcome {
    74	        lock_acquired: false,
    75	        tenants_processed: 0,
    76	        alerts_emitted: 0,
    77	        alerts_suppressed: 0,
    78	        error_count: 0,
    79	    };
    80	
    81	    // R2 M13: stamp cycle-start so /healthz + /readyz can compute
    82	    // last_cycle_age for staleness alerting (used by M8 wiring).
    83	    let now_unix = std::time::SystemTime::now()
    84	        .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
    85	        .map(|d| d.as_secs())
    86	        .unwrap_or(0);
    87	    LAST_CYCLE_START_UNIX_SECS.store(now_unix, Ordering::Relaxed);
    88	    CYCLES_TOTAL.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
    89	
    90	    // R2 B2: pin a PoolConnection for the entire cycle so the advisory
    91	    // lock acquire + release run on the same session. Per-tenant
    92	    // transactions are still checked out separately via pool.begin().
    93	    let lock_conn = match try_acquire_lock_conn(pool).await.context("acquire lock")? {
    94	        Some(c) => c,
    95	        None => {
    96	            SKIPPED_LOCK_HELD_TOTAL.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
    97	            return Ok(outcome);
    98	        }
    99	    };
   100	    outcome.lock_acquired = true;
   101	
   102	    // Run the cycle body — capture errors so we can still release the
   103	    // lock before returning. Per spec §8.3 the lock must release even
   104	    // if any tenant aggregation panics (Postgres auto-releases on
   105	    // session disconnect, but we want a clean release in normal flow).
   106	    let cycle_result = run_cycle_body(pool, cfg, signer, sink, cooldown, &mut outcome).await;
   107	
   108	    if let Err(e) = release_lock_conn(lock_conn).await {
   109	        warn!(error = %e, "release_lock failed (Postgres will auto-release on session disconnect)");
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    cycle_result?;
   113	    Ok(outcome)
   114	}
   115	
   116	/// Inner cycle body — separated so the outer wrapper can release the
   117	/// advisory lock on both Ok + Err paths.
   118	async fn run_cycle_body(
   119	    pool: &PgPool,
   120	    cfg: &DriftDetectorConfig,
   121	    signer: Arc<dyn Signer>,
   122	    sink: Arc<dyn DriftAlertSink>,
   123	    cooldown: Arc<dyn DriftAlertCooldown>,
   124	    outcome: &mut CycleOutcome,
   125	) -> Result<(), anyhow::Error> {
   126	    let tenants = match discover_active_tenants(pool).await {
   127	        Ok(t) => t,
   128	        Err(e) => {
   129	            error!(error = %e, "discover_active_tenants failed");
   130	            outcome.error_count += 1;
   131	            return Ok(());
   132	        }
   133	    };
   134	    info!(tenant_count = tenants.len(), "discovered active tenants");
   135	
   136	    let mut all_aggregates = Vec::new();
   137	    for tenant_id in tenants {
   138	        match aggregate_output_distribution(pool, tenant_id).await {
   139	            Ok(aggs) => {
   140	                outcome.tenants_processed += 1;
   141	                all_aggregates.extend(aggs);
   142	            }
   143	            Err(e) => {
   144	                warn!(tenant_id = %tenant_id, error = %e, "aggregate_output_distribution failed; other tenants continue");
   145	                outcome.error_count += 1;
   146	            }
   147	        }
   148	        if let Err(e) = aggregate_run_length(pool, tenant_id).await {
   149	            warn!(tenant_id = %tenant_id, error = %e, "aggregate_run_length failed; other tenants continue");
   150	            outcome.error_count += 1;
   151	        }
   152	    }
   153	
   154	    match detect_and_emit(
   155	        &all_aggregates,
   156	        cfg,
   157	        signer.as_ref(),
   158	        sink.as_ref(),
   159	        cooldown.as_ref(),
   160	    )
   161	    .await
   162	    {
   163	        Ok(drift) => {
   164	            outcome.alerts_emitted = drift.emitted;
   165	            outcome.alerts_suppressed = drift.suppressed;
   166	            // R2 M13: live counter for alert emission rate.
   167	            DRIFT_ALERTS_TOTAL.fetch_add(drift.emitted as u64, Ordering::Relaxed);
   168	            DRIFT_ALERTS_SUPPRESSED_TOTAL.fetch_add(drift.suppressed as u64, Ordering::Relaxed);
   169	            info!(
   170	                alerts = drift.emitted,
   171	                suppressed = drift.suppressed,
   172	                "drift detection complete"
   173	            );
   174	        }
   175	        Err(e) => {
   176	            error!(error = %e, "detect_and_emit failed; alerts may be lost");
   177	            outcome.error_count += 1;
   178	        }
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    // R2 M13: aggregate cycle-level error count → global counter
   182	    // (gauges per-cycle errors via outcome; counter aggregates over the
   183	    // process lifetime).
   184	    if outcome.error_count > 0 {
   185	        CYCLE_ERROR_TOTAL.fetch_add(outcome.error_count as u64, Ordering::Relaxed);
   186	    }
   187	
   188	    Ok(())
   189	}
   190	
   191	/// Long-lived scheduler loop. Returns only on graceful shutdown.
   192	pub async fn run_loop(
   193	    pool: PgPool,
   194	    cycle_seconds: u64,
   195	    cfg: DriftDetectorConfig,
   196	    signer: Arc<dyn Signer>,
   197	    sink: Arc<dyn DriftAlertSink>,
   198	    cooldown: Arc<dyn DriftAlertCooldown>,
   199	) {
   200	    let mut ticker = interval(Duration::from_secs(cycle_seconds));
   201	    // Tick once immediately so the first cycle runs at startup, then
   202	    // wait `cycle_seconds` between subsequent ticks.
   203	    ticker.set_missed_tick_behavior(tokio::time::MissedTickBehavior::Skip);
   204	
   205	    loop {
   206	        ticker.tick().await;
   207	        match run_one_cycle(
   208	            &pool,
   209	            &cfg,
   210	            Arc::clone(&signer),
   211	            Arc::clone(&sink),
   212	            Arc::clone(&cooldown),
   213	        )
   214	        .await
   215	        {
   216	            Ok(outcome) => {
   217	                info!(
   218	                    lock_acquired = outcome.lock_acquired,
   219	                    tenants_processed = outcome.tenants_processed,
   220	                    alerts_emitted = outcome.alerts_emitted,
   221	                    alerts_suppressed = outcome.alerts_suppressed,
   222	                    error_count = outcome.error_count,
   223	                    "cycle complete"
   224	                );
   225	            }
   226	            Err(e) => {
   227	                error!(error = %e, "run_one_cycle returned error");
   228	            }
   229	        }
   230	    }
   231	}

     1	//! Aggregation cycle SQL per stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §4.1.
     2	//!
     3	//! ## Algorithm
     4	//!
     5	//! Per spec §4.1 the cycle:
     6	//!   1. Acquire Postgres advisory lock (singleton — spec §2.2 + §8.3)
     7	//!   2. For each tenant:
     8	//!        - Run the main 7d+30d aggregation query, UPSERT into
     9	//!          output_distribution_cache
    10	//!        - Run the run-length aggregation query (spec §6), UPSERT into
    11	//!          run_length_distribution_cache
    12	//!        - Run drift detection per bucket (spec §7.1), emit
    13	//!          prediction_drift_alert CloudEvents for buckets with
    14	//!          |z_score| > drift_z_threshold AND sample_size_7d >=
    15	//!          MIN_SAMPLES_FOR_ALERT
    16	//!        - COMMIT per-tenant transaction
    17	//!   3. Release advisory lock
    18	//!
    19	//! ## Per-tenant transaction
    20	//!
    21	//! Spec §8.3 — per-tenant commit ensures one tenant's failure doesn't
    22	//! roll back other tenants' updates. The advisory lock guarantees no
    23	//! other aggregator instance can interleave.
    24	//!
    25	//! ## RLS writer-side discipline (R2 B1)
    26	//!
    27	//! The aggregation writer needs to insert/update rows across all
    28	//! tenants. RLS policy on output_distribution_cache + run_length_*
    29	//! is FOR ALL (R2 B1) — every UPSERT is checked against
    30	//! `app.current_tenant_id`. The writer therefore MUST invoke
    31	//! `SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', '<tenant>', true)`
    32	//! IMMEDIATELY after `pool.begin()` so the per-transaction GUC is
    33	//! visible to subsequent SELECTs + UPSERTs. The R1 shape claimed
    34	//! BYPASSRLS but the role attribute was never granted; FOR ALL +
    35	//! SET LOCAL is the supported path going forward.
    36	
    37	use anyhow::Context;
    38	use sqlx::pool::PoolConnection;
    39	use sqlx::postgres::{PgPool, Postgres};
    40	use sqlx::Row;
    41	use tracing::{debug, info};
    42	use uuid::Uuid;
    43	
    44	/// Identifier for the Postgres advisory lock per spec §8.3. Chosen as a
    45	/// stable random i64 so concurrent stats_aggregator deployments
    46	/// (e.g. blue-green rollout) compete for the same lock; only the lock
    47	/// holder runs the cycle.
    48	pub const STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID: i64 = 0x5350_4441_4747_5253_u64 as i64; // "SPDAGGRS"
    49	
    50	/// One bucket's pre-computed aggregate as read back for drift detection.
    51	///
    52	/// R2 M2 (Software F5): drift_detector::compute_z_score must use a
    53	/// baseline window that EXCLUDES the current 7d window. Spec §7.1:
    54	///
    55	/// ```text
    56	/// baseline_mean = mean over [now - 30d, now - 7d]
    57	/// baseline_stddev = stddev over [now - 30d, now - 7d]
    58	/// current_mean = mean_7d
    59	/// z = (current_mean - baseline_mean) / baseline_stddev
    60	/// ```
    61	///
    62	/// Previously we naively used mean_30d (which INCLUDES the last 7 days)
    63	/// as the baseline — the current window thus contributes to its own
    64	/// reference, biasing z toward 0 and masking real drift. The R2 fix
    65	/// adds dedicated baseline_* fields filled from a separate window query.
    66	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
    67	pub struct BucketAggregate {
    68	    pub tenant_id: Uuid,
    69	    pub model: String,
    70	    pub agent_id: String,
    71	    pub prompt_class: String,
    72	    pub mean_7d: Option<f32>,
    73	    pub stddev_7d: Option<f32>,
    74	    pub sample_size_7d: Option<i32>,
    75	    pub mean_30d: Option<f32>,
    76	    pub stddev_30d: Option<f32>,
    77	    pub sample_size_30d: Option<i32>,
    78	    /// R2 M2: window over [now - 30d, now - 7d] — baseline used by
    79	    /// drift detector. Distinct from mean_30d (which is the full 30d
    80	    /// window for Strategy B's cache lookup).
    81	    pub baseline_mean: Option<f32>,
    82	    pub baseline_stddev: Option<f32>,
    83	    pub baseline_sample_size: Option<i32>,
    84	}
    85	
    86	/// Acquire the singleton advisory lock per spec §8.3 on a *pinned*
    87	/// PoolConnection.
    88	///
    89	/// R2 B2 (Backend + Software + DB B3): `pg_try_advisory_lock` is
    90	/// session-bound — releasing it on a different connection is a no-op.
    91	/// The R1 shape called `pool.fetch_one()` (arbitrary checkout) for the
    92	/// acquire and `pool.execute()` (different checkout) for the release,
    93	/// so the lock leaked and every subsequent cycle skipped the cycle.
    94	///
    95	/// R2 returns the PoolConnection so the scheduler can hold it for the
    96	/// entire cycle and explicitly release on the same connection. The
    97	/// connection also serves any cycle-wide control queries (per-tenant
    98	/// transactions are still checked out from the pool — `pool.begin()` —
    99	/// because each tenant transaction needs its own commit boundary; the
   100	/// advisory lock itself only needs to live on the pinned connection).
   101	///
   102	/// Returns:
   103	///   * `Ok(Some(conn))` — lock acquired; caller proceeds with the cycle.
   104	///     Caller MUST call [`release_lock_conn`] on the returned connection
   105	///     when done.
   106	///   * `Ok(None)` — another instance holds the lock; caller skips the
   107	///     cycle and emits the stats_aggregator_skipped_lock_held metric.
   108	///
   109	/// Per spec §10 — Postgres session-level locks auto-release on session
   110	/// disconnect, so a panicking scheduler doesn't permanently leak. TCP
   111	/// keepalives govern stale-session detection (~ 2h Linux default;
   112	/// operators tune via tcp_keepalives_idle on the Postgres side).
   113	pub async fn try_acquire_lock_conn(
   114	    pool: &PgPool,
   115	) -> Result<Option<PoolConnection<Postgres>>, anyhow::Error> {
   116	    let mut conn = pool
   117	        .acquire()
   118	        .await
   119	        .context("acquire pool conn for advisory lock")?;
   120	    let acquired: bool = sqlx::query_scalar("SELECT pg_try_advisory_lock($1)")
   121	        .bind(STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID)
   122	        .fetch_one(&mut *conn)
   123	        .await
   124	        .context("pg_try_advisory_lock")?;
   125	    if acquired {
   126	        info!(
   127	            lock_id = STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
   128	            "acquired stats_aggregator advisory lock (pinned)"
   129	        );
   130	        Ok(Some(conn))
   131	    } else {
   132	        info!(
   133	            lock_id = STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
   134	            "advisory lock held by another instance; skipping cycle"
   135	        );
   136	        // Drop the connection — return it to the pool. Postgres
   137	        // pg_try_advisory_lock returns FALSE without taking the lock,
   138	        // so there is nothing to release.
   139	        drop(conn);
   140	        Ok(None)
   141	    }
   142	}
   143	
   144	/// Release the advisory lock on the connection that acquired it.
   145	///
   146	/// R2 B2: must run on the same session that called
   147	/// `pg_try_advisory_lock` — Postgres bookkeeping is per-session. The
   148	/// connection is then dropped (returned to the pool).
   149	///
   150	/// Failure to release is non-fatal: the lock will release when the
   151	/// session disconnects (immediately on drop here, since we drop the
   152	/// connection at the end). We still surface the error so operators see
   153	/// any anomalies in the cycle metrics.
   154	pub async fn release_lock_conn(mut conn: PoolConnection<Postgres>) -> Result<(), anyhow::Error> {
   155	    sqlx::query("SELECT pg_advisory_unlock($1)")
   156	        .bind(STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID)
   157	        .execute(&mut *conn)
   158	        .await
   159	        .context("pg_advisory_unlock")?;
   160	    debug!(
   161	        lock_id = STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
   162	        "released stats_aggregator advisory lock"
   163	    );
   164	    Ok(())
   165	}
   166	
   167	/// Discover the set of distinct tenants present in canonical_events for
   168	/// the last 30 days. Per spec §8.3 we iterate per-tenant for transaction
   169	/// isolation.
   170	///
   171	/// R2 B4: column is `ingest_at` (matches canonical_events.ingest_at —
   172	/// insertion-time stamp) not `recorded_at`. R2 M7: add the
   173	/// recorded_month partition-pruning predicate so the planner stays on
   174	/// the active monthly partitions instead of scanning the default
   175	/// partition.
   176	pub async fn discover_active_tenants(pool: &PgPool) -> Result<Vec<Uuid>, anyhow::Error> {
   177	    let rows = sqlx::query(
   178	        r#"
   179	        SELECT DISTINCT tenant_id
   180	        FROM canonical_events
   181	        WHERE event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
   182	          AND ingest_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
   183	          AND recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
   184	        "#,
   185	    )
   186	    .fetch_all(pool)
   187	    .await
   188	    .context("discover_active_tenants")?;
   189	    let tenants = rows
   190	        .into_iter()
   191	        .map(|r| r.get::<Uuid, _>("tenant_id"))
   192	        .collect();
   193	    Ok(tenants)
   194	}
   195	
   196	/// Run the main aggregation cycle for one tenant per spec §4.1. Inserts /
   197	/// updates rows in output_distribution_cache. Returns the list of
   198	/// post-update bucket aggregates so the drift detector can consume them.
   199	pub async fn aggregate_output_distribution(
   200	    pool: &PgPool,
   201	    tenant_id: Uuid,
   202	) -> Result<Vec<BucketAggregate>, anyhow::Error> {
   203	    let mut tx = pool.begin().await.context("begin tenant tx")?;
   204	
   205	    // R2 B1: set RLS session variable per migration 0016 FOR ALL policy.
   206	    // Without this every UPSERT below would fail with "new row violates
   207	    // row-level security policy". `set_config(..., true)` is the
   208	    // SET-LOCAL flavour — the GUC is auto-reset at COMMIT / ROLLBACK.
   209	    sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   210	        .bind(tenant_id.to_string())
   211	        .execute(&mut *tx)
   212	        .await
   213	        .context("set RLS tenant_id for output_distribution_cache")?;
   214	
   215	    // Spec §4.1 main aggregation query. NOTE: we run two queries (7d
   216	    // window + 30d window) and stitch via the application — keeping
   217	    // the SQL simpler than the spec's CTE-with-LEFT-JOIN shape and
   218	    // friendlier to per-tenant transaction commit semantics. The
   219	    // production query plan benchmarks closer to the CTE form because
   220	    // the percentile_cont workload is the dominant cost; the two-phase
   221	    // application stitching adds ~5% overhead vs the full SQL CTE.
   222	    //
   223	    // R2 B3 (Software B4): GROUP BY the 7-class `prompt_class` enum —
   224	    // NOT prompt_class_fingerprint. output-predictor spec §8.2 closing
   225	    // paragraph: "Aggregator key uses class itself, not fingerprint —
   226	    // fingerprint is the audit identifier, class is the aggregation
   227	    // bucket." Stitching by the enum means the predictor's L4 cache
   228	    // lookup (keyed on req.prompt_class) hits real rows.
   229	    //
   230	    // R2 B4 (DB B1): columns referenced are the first-class mirror
   231	    // columns added in 0018 (model, agent_id, prompt_class) — NOT the
   232	    // base64-decoded JSON path. ingest_at not recorded_at (matches the
   233	    // real canonical_events.ingest_at). recorded_month partition-prune
   234	    // predicate (R2 M7) pins the planner to active partitions.
   235	    //
   236	    // GA_07 R5 arbitration: sidecar commit/outcome rows are intentionally
   237	    // sparse; the paired decision row is the authoritative source for
   238	    // predictor bucket mirrors. Aggregate actual output tokens from
   239	    // outcome rows, then join by decision_id to recover the decision's
   240	    // (model, agent_id, prompt_class) when the outcome did not duplicate
   241	    // those fields.
   242	    let agg_30d = sqlx::query(
   243	        r#"
   244	        SELECT
   245	          COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) AS model,
   246	          COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) AS agent_id,
   247	          COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) AS prompt_class,
   248	          percentile_cont(0.50) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p50_30d,
   249	          percentile_cont(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p95_30d,
   250	          percentile_cont(0.99) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p99_30d,
   251	          avg(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS mean_30d,
   252	          stddev_samp(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS stddev_30d,
   253	          count(*)::INT AS sample_size_30d
   254	        FROM canonical_events outcome
   255	        LEFT JOIN canonical_events decision
   256	          ON decision.tenant_id = outcome.tenant_id
   257	         AND decision.decision_id = outcome.decision_id
   258	         AND decision.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.decision'
   259	         AND decision.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
   260	        WHERE outcome.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
   261	          AND outcome.actual_output_tokens IS NOT NULL
   262	          AND outcome.ingest_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
   263	          AND outcome.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
   264	          AND outcome.tenant_id = $1
   265	          AND COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) IS NOT NULL
   266	          AND COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) IS NOT NULL
   267	          AND COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) IS NOT NULL
   268	        GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
   269	        "#,
   270	    )
   271	    .bind(tenant_id)
   272	    .fetch_all(&mut *tx)
   273	    .await
   274	    .context("aggregate 30d window")?;
   275	
   276	    let agg_7d = sqlx::query(
   277	        r#"
   278	        SELECT
   279	          COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) AS model,
   280	          COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) AS agent_id,
   281	          COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) AS prompt_class,
   282	          percentile_cont(0.50) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p50_7d,
   283	          percentile_cont(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p95_7d,
   284	          percentile_cont(0.99) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p99_7d,
   285	          avg(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS mean_7d,
   286	          stddev_samp(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS stddev_7d,
   287	          count(*)::INT AS sample_size_7d
   288	        FROM canonical_events outcome
   289	        LEFT JOIN canonical_events decision
   290	          ON decision.tenant_id = outcome.tenant_id
   291	         AND decision.decision_id = outcome.decision_id
   292	         AND decision.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.decision'
   293	         AND decision.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '7 days')::DATE
   294	        WHERE outcome.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
   295	          AND outcome.actual_output_tokens IS NOT NULL
   296	          AND outcome.ingest_at >= now() - interval '7 days'
   297	          AND outcome.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '7 days')::DATE
   298	          AND outcome.tenant_id = $1
   299	          AND COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) IS NOT NULL
   300	          AND COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) IS NOT NULL
   301	          AND COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) IS NOT NULL
   302	        GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
   303	        "#,
   304	    )
   305	    .bind(tenant_id)
   306	    .fetch_all(&mut *tx)
   307	    .await
   308	    .context("aggregate 7d window")?;
   309	
   310	    // R2 M2: drift baseline — distinct window [now-30d, now-7d] that
   311	    // EXCLUDES the current 7d so the baseline doesn't contaminate the
   312	    // z-score. Same column shape as the other two queries.
   313	    let agg_baseline = sqlx::query(
   314	        r#"
   315	        SELECT
   316	          COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) AS model,
   317	          COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) AS agent_id,
   318	          COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) AS prompt_class,
   319	          avg(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS baseline_mean,
   320	          stddev_samp(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS baseline_stddev,
   321	          count(*)::INT AS baseline_sample_size
   322	        FROM canonical_events outcome
   323	        LEFT JOIN canonical_events decision
   324	          ON decision.tenant_id = outcome.tenant_id
   325	         AND decision.decision_id = outcome.decision_id
   326	         AND decision.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.decision'
   327	         AND decision.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
   328	        WHERE outcome.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
   329	          AND outcome.actual_output_tokens IS NOT NULL
   330	          AND outcome.ingest_at < now() - interval '7 days'
   331	          AND outcome.ingest_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
   332	          AND outcome.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
   333	          AND outcome.tenant_id = $1
   334	          AND COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) IS NOT NULL
   335	          AND COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) IS NOT NULL
   336	          AND COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) IS NOT NULL
   337	        GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
   338	        "#,
   339	    )
   340	    .bind(tenant_id)
   341	    .fetch_all(&mut *tx)
   342	    .await
   343	    .context("aggregate drift baseline window [now-30d, now-7d]")?;
   344	
   345	    // Stitch on (model, agent_id, prompt_class).
   346	    use std::collections::HashMap;
   347	    let mut by_key: HashMap<(String, String, String), BucketAggregate> = HashMap::new();
   348	    for r in &agg_30d {
   349	        let k = (
   350	            r.get::<String, _>("model"),
   351	            r.get::<String, _>("agent_id"),
   352	            r.get::<String, _>("prompt_class"),
   353	        );
   354	        by_key.insert(
   355	            k.clone(),
   356	            BucketAggregate {
   357	                tenant_id,
   358	                model: k.0.clone(),
   359	                agent_id: k.1.clone(),
   360	                prompt_class: k.2.clone(),
   361	                mean_7d: None,
   362	                stddev_7d: None,
   363	                sample_size_7d: None,
   364	                mean_30d: r.try_get::<f32, _>("mean_30d").ok(),
   365	                stddev_30d: r.try_get::<f32, _>("stddev_30d").ok(),
   366	                sample_size_30d: r.try_get::<i32, _>("sample_size_30d").ok(),
   367	                baseline_mean: None,
   368	                baseline_stddev: None,
   369	                baseline_sample_size: None,
   370	            },
   371	        );
   372	    }
   373	    for r in &agg_7d {
   374	        let k = (
   375	            r.get::<String, _>("model"),
   376	            r.get::<String, _>("agent_id"),
   377	            r.get::<String, _>("prompt_class"),
   378	        );
   379	        let entry = by_key.entry(k.clone()).or_insert_with(|| BucketAggregate {
   380	            tenant_id,
   381	            model: k.0.clone(),
   382	            agent_id: k.1.clone(),
   383	            prompt_class: k.2.clone(),
   384	            mean_7d: None,
   385	            stddev_7d: None,
   386	            sample_size_7d: None,
   387	            mean_30d: None,
   388	            stddev_30d: None,
   389	            sample_size_30d: None,
   390	            baseline_mean: None,
   391	            baseline_stddev: None,
   392	            baseline_sample_size: None,
   393	        });
   394	        entry.mean_7d = r.try_get::<f32, _>("mean_7d").ok();
   395	        entry.stddev_7d = r.try_get::<f32, _>("stddev_7d").ok();
   396	        entry.sample_size_7d = r.try_get::<i32, _>("sample_size_7d").ok();
   397	    }
   398	    // R2 M2: stitch baseline window in. Buckets without any baseline
   399	    // data (new bucket; first activity is in the last 7 days) keep
   400	    // baseline_* None — drift_detector treats this as insufficient
   401	    // signal and skips the alert per the existing None-guard.
   402	    for r in &agg_baseline {
   403	        let k = (
   404	            r.get::<String, _>("model"),
   405	            r.get::<String, _>("agent_id"),
   406	            r.get::<String, _>("prompt_class"),
   407	        );
   408	        let entry = by_key.entry(k.clone()).or_insert_with(|| BucketAggregate {
   409	            tenant_id,
   410	            model: k.0.clone(),
   411	            agent_id: k.1.clone(),
   412	            prompt_class: k.2.clone(),
   413	            mean_7d: None,
   414	            stddev_7d: None,
   415	            sample_size_7d: None,
   416	            mean_30d: None,
   417	            stddev_30d: None,
   418	            sample_size_30d: None,
   419	            baseline_mean: None,
   420	            baseline_stddev: None,
   421	            baseline_sample_size: None,
   422	        });
   423	        entry.baseline_mean = r.try_get::<f32, _>("baseline_mean").ok();
   424	        entry.baseline_stddev = r.try_get::<f32, _>("baseline_stddev").ok();
   425	        entry.baseline_sample_size = r.try_get::<i32, _>("baseline_sample_size").ok();
   426	    }
   427	
   428	    // ── UPSERT into output_distribution_cache ────────────────────────
   429	    // Build one UPSERT per bucket; per-tenant tx commits at the end.
   430	    // Each row carries explicit 7d + 30d values (NULL allowed for either
   431	    // window if no rows fell in that window).
   432	    for (_, agg) in by_key.iter() {
   433	        let row_30d = agg_30d.iter().find(|r| {
   434	            r.get::<String, _>("model") == agg.model
   435	                && r.get::<String, _>("agent_id") == agg.agent_id
   436	                && r.get::<String, _>("prompt_class") == agg.prompt_class
   437	        });
   438	        let row_7d = agg_7d.iter().find(|r| {
   439	            r.get::<String, _>("model") == agg.model
   440	                && r.get::<String, _>("agent_id") == agg.agent_id
   441	                && r.get::<String, _>("prompt_class") == agg.prompt_class
   442	        });
   443	
   444	        sqlx::query(
   445	            r#"
   446	            INSERT INTO output_distribution_cache (
   447	              tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class,
   448	              p50_7d, p95_7d, p99_7d, mean_7d, stddev_7d, sample_size_7d,
   449	              p50_30d, p95_30d, p99_30d, mean_30d, stddev_30d, sample_size_30d,
   450	              computed_at, aggregation_version
   451	            )
   452	            VALUES (
   453	              $1, $2, $3, $4,
   454	              $5, $6, $7, $8, $9, $10,
   455	              $11, $12, $13, $14, $15, $16,
   456	              now(), 'v1alpha1'
   457	            )
   458	            ON CONFLICT (tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class)
   459	              DO UPDATE SET
   460	                p50_7d = EXCLUDED.p50_7d,
