     9	--
    10	-- ## Purpose
    11	--
    12	-- Per spec §6 the stats_aggregator computes per-(tenant, agent_id) historical
    13	-- P95 run length (steps per run) on the same hourly cadence as the output
    14	-- distribution cache. The run_cost_projector (SLICE_09) consumes this for
    15	-- Signal 1 cost projection. SLICE_06 lands the schema; SLICE_09 wires the

    17	--
    18	-- ## Why a separate table
    19	--

    22	-- Co-located in canonical_ingest DB for the same locality reason as 0016.
    23	--
    24	-- ## Privilege boundary + RLS

    30	-- canonical_ingest_reader_role gets SELECT.
    31	--
    32	-- ## Stylistic alignment
    33	--
    34	-- - psql autocommit per SLICE_01 R5

    42	    -- or prompt_class because run length is per-agent semantic property
    43	    -- not per-call semantic property.
    44	    tenant_id            UUID NOT NULL,
    45	    agent_id             TEXT NOT NULL,
    46

    48	    -- is SLICE-extra; 7d window not needed for v1alpha1).

    50	    p95_steps_30d        REAL,
    51	    p99_steps_30d        REAL,
    52	    mean_steps_30d       REAL,
    53	    stddev_steps_30d     REAL,
    54	    sample_size_30d      INTEGER CHECK (sample_size_30d IS NULL OR sample_size_30d >= 0),
    55	
    56	    -- Metadata. TZ-explicit +00 per SLICE_01 R5. R2 M17: no DEFAULT on
    57	    -- computed_at — writer always supplies explicit `now()` (matches
    58	    -- 0016 convention; closes the same in-transaction freshness foot-gun).
    59	    computed_at          TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    60	    aggregation_version  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'v1alpha1',
    61

    63	);

    73	ALTER TABLE run_length_distribution_cache FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
    74

    76	    ON run_length_distribution_cache
    77	    FOR ALL
    78	    USING (
    79	        tenant_id = COALESCE(

   100	    ON run_length_distribution_cache

   170	/// Long-lived scheduler loop. Returns only on graceful shutdown.
   171	pub async fn run_loop(
   172	    pool: PgPool,
   173	    cycle_seconds: u64,
   174	    cfg: DriftDetectorConfig,
   175	    signer: Arc<dyn Signer>,
   176	    sink: Arc<dyn DriftAlertSink>,
   177	) {
   178	    let mut ticker = interval(Duration::from_secs(cycle_seconds));
   179	    // Tick once immediately so the first cycle runs at startup, then
   180	    // wait `cycle_seconds` between subsequent ticks.
   181	    ticker.set_missed_tick_behavior(tokio::time::MissedTickBehavior::Skip);
   182	
   183	    loop {
   184	        ticker.tick().await;
   185	        match run_one_cycle(&pool, &cfg, Arc::clone(&signer), Arc::clone(&sink)).await {
   186	            Ok(outcome) => {
   187	                info!(
   188	                    lock_acquired = outcome.lock_acquired,
   189	                    tenants_processed = outcome.tenants_processed,
   190	                    alerts_emitted = outcome.alerts_emitted,

     1	-- ============================================================================
     2	-- 0016_output_distribution_cache.sql — Stats Aggregator Strategy B cache.
     3	--
     4	-- Spec ancestors:
     5	--   - docs/stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §5 (authoritative DDL)
     6	--   - docs/stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §3.2 (bucket key)
     7	--   - docs/stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §9 (multi-tenant isolation)
     8	--   - docs/slices/SLICE_06_output_predictor_a_b_stats_aggregator.md §5
     9	--   - docs/output-predictor-service-spec-v1alpha1.md §4 (B cache consumer)
    10	--
    11	-- ## Why this table lives in canonical_ingest DB
    12	--
    13	-- Spec §3.1 — stats_aggregator reads `canonical_events` and writes the
    14	-- pre-computed P50/P95/P99 cache. Co-locating the cache with the source
    15	-- canonical_events table eliminates the cross-DB lookup the output_predictor
    16	-- would otherwise incur. Reader: output_predictor connects directly to
    17	-- canonical_ingest DB read-only (per spec §4.2 read-only connection pool).
    18	--
    19	-- ## Why NOT partitioned (spec §5.1)
    20	--
    21	-- Scale estimate per spec: 1000 tenants × 20 models × 50 agents × 7 classes
    22	-- ≈ 7M rows max. ON CONFLICT UPSERT performs well at that scale; partition
    23	-- pruning + cross-partition uniqueness costs outweigh the benefit.
    24	-- Re-partition by `(tenant_id % 256)` if production scales beyond 50K
    25	-- tenants (post-launch decision, tracked in spec §5.1).
    26	--
    27	-- Mutability: this is a derived/cache table — operators may TRUNCATE +
    28	-- rebuild from canonical_events. No immutability trigger. No verify-chain
    29	-- coverage (verify-chain audits canonical_events directly).
    30	--
    31	-- ## Privilege boundary
    32	--
    33	-- Mirrors 0005_immutability_triggers.sql roles:
    34	--   - canonical_ingest_application_role: aggregation writer + reader (stats_aggregator)
    35	--   - canonical_ingest_reader_role: read-only (output_predictor + calibration)
    36	--
    37	-- DELETE granted to application role for retention / rebuild cycles.
    38	-- UPDATE granted because the aggregation cycle UPSERTs (spec §4.3).
    39	--
    40	-- ## Stylistic alignment
    41	--
    42	-- - psql autocommit per SLICE_01 R5 (each statement commits independently)
    43	-- - SET LOCAL search_path = pg_catalog, pg_temp in DO blocks (CVE-2018-1058
    44	--   hardening per SLICE_01 R5)
    45	-- - TIMESTAMPTZ with TZ-explicit `+00` per SLICE_01 R5
    46	-- - No down migration file per SLICE_03 R2 M3 convention; rollback via
    47	--   `DROP TABLE output_distribution_cache CASCADE` (operator one-liner)
    48	--
    49	-- ## Multi-tenant isolation (spec §9)
    50	--
    51	-- Row-Level Security ON with FOR ALL policy: every SELECT and every
    52	-- INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE requires the caller's session to have
    53	-- `SET LOCAL app.current_tenant_id = '<uuid>'` before the query.
    54	--
    55	-- ### R2 B1 — writer path correction
    56	--
    57	-- R1 prior shape declared `FOR SELECT` + claimed `BYPASSRLS` for the
    58	-- aggregation writer, but BYPASSRLS was never granted to the application
    59	-- role (no GRANT BYPASSRLS in this migration; no role-level attribute in
    60	-- 0005_immutability_triggers.sql). Under FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY the
    61	-- writer's UPSERTs would be rejected with
    62	-- "new row violates row-level security policy". R2 widens the policy to
    63	-- FOR ALL and pairs it with the writer's SET LOCAL discipline (see
    64	-- services/stats_aggregator/src/aggregation.rs::aggregate_output_distribution
    65	-- — invokes `set_config('app.current_tenant_id', tenant, true)` before
    66	-- every per-tenant UPSERT). Reader path (output_predictor cache.rs) sets
    67	-- the same variable for SELECT. Same contract, no BYPASSRLS dependency.
    68	-- ============================================================================
    69	
    70	CREATE TABLE output_distribution_cache (
    71	    -- Bucket key (per spec §3.2 + §5). Tenant UUID per the rest of the
    72	    -- ledger schema convention (0003 budget_window_instances etc.). Model
    73	    -- + agent_id + prompt_class are opaque application-defined identifiers;
    74	    -- TEXT to remain bytes-clean for non-Latin model strings.
    75	    tenant_id            UUID NOT NULL,
    76	    model                TEXT NOT NULL,
    77	    agent_id             TEXT NOT NULL,
    78	    prompt_class         TEXT NOT NULL,
    79	
    80	    -- 7-day rolling window (per spec §4.2 drift detection signal)
    81	    p50_7d               REAL,
    82	    p95_7d               REAL,
    83	    p99_7d               REAL,
    84	    mean_7d              REAL,
    85	    stddev_7d            REAL,
    86	    sample_size_7d       INTEGER CHECK (sample_size_7d IS NULL OR sample_size_7d >= 0),
    87	
    88	    -- 30-day rolling window (per spec §4.2 Strategy B baseline)
    89	    p50_30d              REAL,
    90	    p95_30d              REAL,
    91	    p99_30d              REAL,
    92	    mean_30d             REAL,
    93	    stddev_30d           REAL,
    94	    sample_size_30d      INTEGER CHECK (sample_size_30d IS NULL OR sample_size_30d >= 0),
    95	
    96	    -- Metadata. computed_at TZ-explicit +00 per SLICE_01 R5 convention.
    97	    -- aggregation_version lets downstream consumers detect SQL aggregation
    98	    -- recipe changes (spec §0.1 compatibility policy "aggregation_version
    99	    -- column versioned").
   100	    --
   101	    -- R2 M17: no DEFAULT on computed_at — the aggregation writer ALWAYS
   102	    -- supplies an explicit `now()`. Removing the default closes a foot-gun
   103	    -- where an ad-hoc INSERT could land with `clock_timestamp()` from
   104	    -- within a long-running transaction (the freshness gate downstream
   105	    -- relies on the writer-supplied stamp being the real cycle time).
   106	    computed_at          TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
   107	    aggregation_version  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'v1alpha1',
   108	
   109	    PRIMARY KEY (tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class)
   110	);
   111	
   112	-- Freshness lookup: "find buckets where computed_at < cutoff" supports
   113	-- both the SLO freshness alert and the rebuild trigger.
   114	CREATE INDEX output_distribution_cache_freshness_idx
   115	    ON output_distribution_cache (computed_at);
   116	
   117	-- Tenant lookup index — Strategy B hot-path query (per spec §4.2).
   118	-- Covers the most-common WHERE shape (tenant_id, model, agent_id,
   119	-- prompt_class). PRIMARY KEY already covers (tenant_id, model,
   120	-- agent_id, prompt_class) so this index is redundant for equality;
   121	-- kept commented to document the access pattern — the optimiser
   122	-- uses the PK btree directly.
   123	-- CREATE INDEX output_distribution_cache_tenant_lookup_idx ...
   124	
   125	-- ============================================================================
   126	-- Row-Level Security (spec §9.1 mechanism 1).
   127	--
   128	-- Policy: `tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::uuid`
   129	-- means the calling session MUST have run
   130	-- `SET LOCAL app.current_tenant_id = '<uuid>'` inside its transaction
   131	-- before the SELECT. output_predictor::cache.rs does this per Predict
   132	-- call. Operators querying ad-hoc via psql see 0 rows until they set
   133	-- the session variable explicitly.
   134	--
   135	-- R2 B1 fix: writer uses `set_config('app.current_tenant_id', ...)` per
   136	-- tenant before UPSERT — the policy's WITH CHECK clause then enforces
   137	-- tenant_id matches the session variable at INSERT/UPDATE. No BYPASSRLS
   138	-- attribute on the role; defense-in-depth via FORCE RLS. Adversarial
   139	-- cross-tenant query injection (per spec §9.2) is blocked by the policy
   140	-- + session variable contract for both reads and writes.
   141	-- ============================================================================
   142	
   143	ALTER TABLE output_distribution_cache ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
   144	ALTER TABLE output_distribution_cache FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
   145	
   146	-- R2 B1: FOR ALL policy. SELECT path enforces USING; INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE
   147	-- additionally enforces WITH CHECK so a writer who forgets the SET LOCAL
   148	-- still fails closed (cannot insert a row with mismatched tenant_id).
   149	--
   150	-- Use COALESCE to a deliberately-illegal sentinel so a missing session
   151	-- variable produces a clean tenant-mismatch (returns 0 rows / rejects
   152	-- WITH CHECK) rather than silently leaking every tenant's rows under a
   153	-- NULL match. The sentinel '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000' is
   154	-- the nil UUID which never matches any production tenant_id (all
   155	-- tenants mint UUIDv7 with timestamp > 0).
   156	CREATE POLICY output_distribution_cache_tenant_isolation
   157	    ON output_distribution_cache
   158	    FOR ALL
   159	    USING (
   160	        tenant_id = COALESCE(
   161	            NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_tenant_id', TRUE), ''),
   162	            '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000'
   163	        )::uuid
   164	    )
   165	    WITH CHECK (
   166	        tenant_id = COALESCE(
   167	            NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_tenant_id', TRUE), ''),
   168	            '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000'
   169	        )::uuid
   170	    );
   171	
   172	-- ============================================================================
   173	-- Privilege boundary (mirror of 0005_immutability_triggers.sql convention).
   174	--
   175	-- canonical_ingest_application_role: stats_aggregator (writer) +
   176	--   output_predictor pool (reader path goes through application role to
   177	--   pick up RLS — reader role bypasses RLS by default which is wrong here).
   178	-- canonical_ingest_reader_role: ad-hoc operator queries. RLS applies.
   179	--
   180	-- R2 M16: REVOKE SELECT FROM PUBLIC. Without it, any new connecting role
   181	-- inherits PUBLIC's SELECT and can run cross-tenant probes through the
   182	-- RLS policy. Belt-and-suspenders on top of RLS — defence in depth.
   183	-- ============================================================================
   184	
   185	REVOKE SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE ON output_distribution_cache FROM PUBLIC;
   186	
   187	GRANT SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
   188	    ON output_distribution_cache
   189	    TO canonical_ingest_application_role;
   190	
   191	GRANT SELECT ON output_distribution_cache TO canonical_ingest_reader_role;
   192	
   193	COMMENT ON TABLE output_distribution_cache IS
   194	    'Strategy B per-(tenant, model, agent_id, prompt_class) P50/P95/P99 distribution cache per stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §5. Populated hourly by services/stats_aggregator. Read by services/output_predictor on the Predict hot path. RLS FOR ALL policy enforces per-tenant isolation at both read AND write time; the stats_aggregator writer SETs app.current_tenant_id per tenant before each UPSERT (R2 B1). Mutable (UPSERT every cycle); no immutability trigger.';
   195	COMMENT ON COLUMN output_distribution_cache.tenant_id IS
   196	    'Tenant identifier (UUIDv7). Indexed via PRIMARY KEY for hot-path Predict lookup.';
   197	COMMENT ON COLUMN output_distribution_cache.computed_at IS
   198	    'Last successful aggregation cycle timestamp. Stale > 2h treated as cache miss by output_predictor per output-predictor-service-spec-v1alpha1.md §4.2.';
   199	COMMENT ON COLUMN output_distribution_cache.aggregation_version IS
   200	    'Aggregation recipe version; rows produced by older recipes can be invalidated by output_predictor when the spec version bumps.';
   201	
   202	-- ============================================================================
   203	-- DO-block smoke check: verify RLS is actually enabled and the policy
   204	-- exists. CVE-2018-1058 hardening: SET LOCAL search_path so PostgreSQL
   205	-- resolves built-in catalog names (pg_catalog.pg_class etc.) without
   206	-- consulting a search_path that an adversary might have injected
   207	-- (per SLICE_01 R5).
   208	-- ============================================================================
   209	DO $$
   210	BEGIN
   211	    SET LOCAL search_path = pg_catalog, pg_temp;
   212	    PERFORM 1 FROM pg_class
   213	        WHERE relname = 'output_distribution_cache' AND relrowsecurity = TRUE;
   214	    IF NOT FOUND THEN
   215	        RAISE EXCEPTION 'output_distribution_cache RLS not enabled after migration';
   216	    END IF;
   217	    PERFORM 1 FROM pg_policy
   218	        WHERE polname = 'output_distribution_cache_tenant_isolation';
   219	    IF NOT FOUND THEN
   220	        RAISE EXCEPTION 'output_distribution_cache_tenant_isolation policy missing';
   221	    END IF;
   222	END $$;

codex
The core cooldown path now checks before emit and records after append, which matches the documented failure-mode tradeoff. I’m looking for subtler production gaps now: deployment compatibility, RLS edge cases, non-finite JSON serialization, and whether the added tests actually exercise the runtime path rather than only the store abstraction.

     1	-- Canonical events mirror of the audit_outbox prediction columns added
     2	-- in services/ledger/migrations/0046_audit_outbox_prediction_columns.sql.
     3	--
     4	-- Spec ancestor: docs/audit-chain-prediction-extension-v1alpha1.md §6 +
     5	-- SLICE_01 §2 ("Add columns to canonical_events table — mirror schema;
     6	-- replicated via outbox_forwarder unchanged").
     7	--
     8	-- Why mirror to canonical_events:
     9	--   * calibration-report CLI runs SQL aggregations against canonical_events
    10	--     (the storage-class-bound canonical store; audit_outbox is the
    11	--     ledger-side outbox the forwarder replicates from).
    12	--   * cross-storage consistency check (spec §11.2 + verify-chain
    13	--     --check-prediction-mirror) compares column values between
    14	--     audit_outbox and canonical_events; symmetric schema is required.
    15	--   * payload_json continues to carry the CloudEvent envelope including
    16	--     proto fields 300-317, so the canonical signature still covers them
    17	--     end-to-end; the first-class columns are SQL accelerators.
    18	--
    19	-- All ADD COLUMN nullable. No backfill — legacy rows stay NULL. The
    20	-- existing canonical_events_no_update_delete trigger (BEFORE UPDATE OR
    21	-- DELETE; round-2 fix m1 — name corrected from prior round-1 comment
    22	-- "canonical_events_immutability") already rejects ALL mutations on
    23	-- canonical_events, so no trigger update is needed here — the table is
    24	-- strictly append-only at the application level. Adding NULLable columns
    25	-- is a metadata-only operation on the partitioned parent; child
    26	-- partitions inherit instantaneously.
    27	--
    28	-- The outbox_forwarder path is unchanged: it reads audit_outbox columns
    29	-- and the CloudEvent payload, pushes via gRPC AppendEvents, and
    30	-- canonical_ingest's persistence layer (services/canonical_ingest/src/
    31	-- persistence/append.rs) populates the first-class mirror columns
    32	-- starting in SLICE_06 along with the proto field mirror in producers.
    33	--
    34	-- Cross-DB deployment ordering (round-2 fix M16): this migration MUST
    35	-- run AFTER services/ledger/migrations/0046+0048 because the spec §6
    36	-- mirror invariant requires the ledger side to be schema-ready first.
    37	-- The Helm migrations.yaml apply loop enforces this by processing the
    38	-- ledger glob before the canonical glob.
    39	--
    40	-- Migration runner wrapping convention: no explicit BEGIN/COMMIT — the
    41	-- runner wraps each .sql in its own transaction (round-2 fix m3,
    42	-- matches the 12 pre-existing canonical_ingest migrations 0000-0012).
    43	
    44	-- ============================================================================
    45	-- Step 1: Add the 18 new columns. INT → BIGINT for token-count columns
    46	-- per round-2 finding M4. prediction_confidence NUMERIC(4,3) per M12.
    47	-- ============================================================================
    48	
    49	ALTER TABLE canonical_events
    50	    -- === Decision-side prediction columns (11 total per spec §2.1) ===
    51	    ADD COLUMN predicted_a_tokens         BIGINT,
    52	    ADD COLUMN predicted_b_tokens         BIGINT,
    53	    ADD COLUMN predicted_c_tokens         BIGINT,
    54	    ADD COLUMN reserved_strategy          TEXT,
    55	    ADD COLUMN prediction_strategy_used   TEXT,
    56	    ADD COLUMN prediction_policy_used     TEXT,
    57	    ADD COLUMN tokenizer_tier             TEXT,
    58	    ADD COLUMN tokenizer_version_id       UUID,
    59	    ADD COLUMN prediction_confidence      NUMERIC(4,3),
    60	    ADD COLUMN prediction_sample_size     BIGINT,
    61	    ADD COLUMN cold_start_layer_used      TEXT,
    62	
    63	    -- === Run-level projection columns (3 total per spec §2.2) ===
    64	    ADD COLUMN run_projection_at_decision_atomic NUMERIC(38,0),
    65	    ADD COLUMN run_predicted_remaining_steps     INT,
    66	    ADD COLUMN run_steps_completed_so_far        BIGINT,
    67	
    68	    -- === Commit-side actual columns (4 total per spec §2.3) ===
    69	    ADD COLUMN actual_input_tokens   BIGINT,
    70	    ADD COLUMN actual_output_tokens  BIGINT,
    71	    ADD COLUMN delta_b_ratio         REAL,
    72	    ADD COLUMN delta_c_ratio         REAL;
    73	
    74	-- ============================================================================
    75	-- Step 2: Domain CHECK constraints — mirror of ledger side
    76	-- (round-2 fixes M2 / M3 / M5 / M6 / M12).
    77	-- ============================================================================
    78	
    79	ALTER TABLE canonical_events
    80	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_reserved_strategy_chk
    81	        CHECK (reserved_strategy IS NULL OR reserved_strategy IN ('A','B','C'))
    82	        NOT VALID,
    83	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_strategy_used_chk
    84	        CHECK (prediction_strategy_used IS NULL
    85	               OR prediction_strategy_used IN ('A','B','C'))
    86	        NOT VALID,
    87	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_policy_used_chk
    88	        CHECK (prediction_policy_used IS NULL OR prediction_policy_used IN (
    89	            'STRICT_CEILING','EMPIRICAL_RUN_CEILING',
    90	            'ADAPTIVE_CEILING','SHADOW_ONLY'))
    91	        NOT VALID,
    92	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_tokenizer_tier_chk
    93	        CHECK (tokenizer_tier IS NULL OR tokenizer_tier IN ('T1','T2','T3'))
    94	        NOT VALID,
    95	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_confidence_chk
    96	        CHECK (prediction_confidence IS NULL
    97	               OR (prediction_confidence >= 0.000
    98	                   AND prediction_confidence <= 1.000))
    99	        NOT VALID,
   100	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_cold_start_layer_used_chk
   101	        CHECK (cold_start_layer_used IS NULL
   102	               OR cold_start_layer_used IN ('L1','L2','L3','L4'))
   103	        NOT VALID,
   104	
   105	    -- === Sentinel discipline mirror (round-2 fix M3) ===
   106	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_predicted_tokens_chk
   107	        CHECK ((predicted_a_tokens IS NULL OR predicted_a_tokens >= 0)
   108	           AND (predicted_b_tokens IS NULL OR predicted_b_tokens >= 0)
   109	           AND (predicted_c_tokens IS NULL OR predicted_c_tokens >= 0))
   110	        NOT VALID,
   111	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_actual_tokens_chk
   112	        CHECK ((actual_input_tokens IS NULL OR actual_input_tokens >= 0)
   113	           AND (actual_output_tokens IS NULL OR actual_output_tokens >= 0))
   114	        NOT VALID,
   115	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_run_steps_chk
   116	        CHECK ((run_predicted_remaining_steps IS NULL
   117	                  OR run_predicted_remaining_steps >= -1)
   118	           AND (run_steps_completed_so_far IS NULL
   119	                  OR run_steps_completed_so_far >= 0))
   120	        NOT VALID,
   121	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_run_projection_chk
   122	        CHECK (run_projection_at_decision_atomic IS NULL
   123	               OR run_projection_at_decision_atomic >= 0)
   124	        NOT VALID,
   125	    -- Round-2 fix M5 mirror: int64 overflow guard for proto field 311.
   126	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_run_projection_int64_chk
   127	        CHECK (run_projection_at_decision_atomic IS NULL
   128	               OR run_projection_at_decision_atomic <= 9223372036854775807)
   129	        NOT VALID,
   130	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_sample_size_chk
   131	        CHECK (prediction_sample_size IS NULL OR prediction_sample_size >= 0)
   132	        NOT VALID,
   133	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_delta_b_ratio_chk
   134	        CHECK (delta_b_ratio IS NULL
   135	               OR (delta_b_ratio >= 0.0 AND delta_b_ratio = delta_b_ratio))
   136	        NOT VALID,
   137	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_delta_c_ratio_chk
   138	        CHECK (delta_c_ratio IS NULL
   139	               OR (delta_c_ratio >= 0.0 AND delta_c_ratio = delta_c_ratio))
   140	        NOT VALID;
   141	
   142	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_reserved_strategy_chk;
   143	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_strategy_used_chk;
   144	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_policy_used_chk;
   145	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_tokenizer_tier_chk;
   146	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_confidence_chk;
   147	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_cold_start_layer_used_chk;
   148	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_predicted_tokens_chk;
   149	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_actual_tokens_chk;
   150	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_run_steps_chk;
   151	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_run_projection_chk;
   152	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_run_projection_int64_chk;
   153	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prediction_sample_size_chk;
   154	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_delta_b_ratio_chk;
   155	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_delta_c_ratio_chk;
   156	
   157	-- ============================================================================
   158	-- Step 3: Partial NOT-NULL via CHECK on event_type (round-2 fix M2
   159	-- mirror of ledger side, per spec §2.1-§2.3 "Nullable: NO" columns).
   160	--
   161	-- The same event_time < '2027-01-01' cutoff applies (round-3 fix B5:
   162	-- extended from 2026-07-01 calendar bomb) — SLICE_06 producers begin
   163	-- populating these columns; SLICE_06 deployment plan MUST land before
   164	-- 2027-01-01.
   165	--
   166	-- Round-4 fix B4: DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS prepended so re-application
   167	-- against a database that previously ran the 2026-07-01 form replaces
   168	-- the CHECK body cleanly. Same-name + different body would error 42710
   169	-- or silently keep the old body. Drop-then-add inside the same
   170	-- migration-runner transaction keeps observers in a consistent state.
   171	-- ============================================================================
   172	
   173	ALTER TABLE canonical_events
   174	    DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS canonical_events_decision_required_cols_chk,
   175	    DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS canonical_events_outcome_required_cols_chk;
   176	
   177	ALTER TABLE canonical_events
   178	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_decision_required_cols_chk
   179	        CHECK (event_type <> 'spendguard.audit.decision'
   180	               OR event_time < '2027-01-01 00:00:00+00'::timestamptz
   181	               OR (predicted_a_tokens IS NOT NULL
   182	                   AND reserved_strategy IS NOT NULL
   183	                   AND prediction_strategy_used IS NOT NULL
   184	                   AND prediction_policy_used IS NOT NULL
   185	                   AND tokenizer_tier IS NOT NULL
   186	                   AND run_projection_at_decision_atomic IS NOT NULL
   187	                   AND run_steps_completed_so_far IS NOT NULL))
   188	        NOT VALID,
   189	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_outcome_required_cols_chk
   190	        CHECK (event_type <> 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
   191	               OR event_time < '2027-01-01 00:00:00+00'::timestamptz
   192	               OR (actual_input_tokens IS NOT NULL
   193	                   AND actual_output_tokens IS NOT NULL))
   194	        NOT VALID;
   195	
   196	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_decision_required_cols_chk;
   197	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_outcome_required_cols_chk;
   198

     1	//! `CanonicalIngest::AppendEvents` handler.
     2	//!
     3	//! Per Stage 2 §8.2.2 + Trace §10.1 / §10.2 / §13:
     4	//!   * Verify producer signature (TODO: keys come from sidecar handshake).
     5	//!   * Verify schema_bundle exists + hash matches.
     6	//!   * For each event in batch:
     7	//!       1) Dedupe by event_id; on collision return `DEDUPED`.
     8	//!       2) Classify storage_class from event_type (Trace §10.2).
     9	//!       3) For audit.outcome:
    10	//!           - check matching audit.decision exists; if not → quarantine,
    11	//!             return `AWAITING_PRECEDING_DECISION`.
    12	//!       4) For all other events: append atomically to canonical_events +
    13	//!          canonical_events_global_keys.
    14	//!   * On backpressure (quarantine depth > threshold): enforcement-route
    15	//!     events fail_closed; observability-route events still buffer.
    16	//!
    17	//! POC simplifications:
    18	//!   * Producer signature verification is stubbed (TODO: integrate with
    19	//!     sidecar Producer Trust §13).
    20	//!   * Each event runs in its own Postgres transaction. Batch atomicity is
    21	//!     not required by spec; per-event independent results are.
    22	
    23	use bigdecimal::BigDecimal;
    24	use chrono::Utc;
    25	use prost_types::Timestamp;
    26	use sha2::{Digest, Sha256};
    27	use spendguard_signing::{Verifier, VerifyFailure};
    28	use sqlx::PgPool;
    29	use std::str::FromStr;
    30	use tracing::{debug, instrument, warn};
    31	use uuid::Uuid;
    32	
    33	use crate::{
    34	    config::Config,
    35	    domain::{error::DomainError, event_routing::classify},
    36	    metrics::{IngestMetrics, QuarantineReason, Route as MetricsRoute},
    37	    persistence::{
    38	        append::{self, AppendInput, AppendOutcome},
    39	        query, schema_bundle, signature_quarantine,
    40	    },
    41	    proto::{
    42	        canonical_ingest::v1::{
    43	            AppendEventsRequest, AppendEventsResponse, EventResult, IngestPosition,
    44	            append_events_request::Route, event_result::Status as EventStatus,
    45	        },
    46	        common::v1::{CloudEvent, Error as ProtoError, error::Code as ProtoCode},
    47	    },
    48	    verifier::canonical_bytes,
    49	};
    50	
    51	#[instrument(skip(pool, cfg, verifier, metrics, req), fields(
    52	    producer_id = %req.producer_id,
    53	    event_count = req.events.len(),
    54	    route = ?req.route()
    55	))]
    56	pub async fn handle(
    57	    pool: &PgPool,
    58	    cfg: &Config,
    59	    verifier: Option<&dyn Verifier>,
    60	    metrics: &IngestMetrics,
    61	    req: AppendEventsRequest,
    62	) -> Result<AppendEventsResponse, tonic::Status> {
    63	    // Validate batch envelope.
    64	    if req.producer_id.is_empty() {
    65	        return Err(tonic::Status::invalid_argument("producer_id required"));
    66	    }
    67	    if req.events.is_empty() {
    68	        return Err(tonic::Status::invalid_argument("events must not be empty"));
    69	    }
    70	    let bundle_ref = req
    71	        .schema_bundle
    72	        .as_ref()
    73	        .ok_or_else(|| tonic::Status::invalid_argument("schema_bundle required"))?;
    74	
    75	    // Reject ROUTE_UNSPECIFIED before touching storage. The route is part
    76	    // of the batch envelope and must fail closed even if the schema bundle
    77	    // would otherwise be unknown.
    78	    let route = req.route();
    79	    if route == Route::Unspecified {
    80	        return Err(tonic::Status::invalid_argument(
    81	            "route is unspecified; clients MUST set ENFORCEMENT or OBSERVABILITY",
    82	        ));
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    // Verify schema bundle existence + hash.
    86	    let bundle_id = parse_uuid(
    87	        &bundle_ref.schema_bundle_id,
    88	        "schema_bundle.schema_bundle_id",
    89	    )
    90	    .map_err(|e| e.to_status())?;
    91	    let bundle = match schema_bundle::lookup(pool, bundle_id, &bundle_ref.schema_bundle_hash).await
    92	    {
    93	        Ok(Some(b)) => b,
    94	        Ok(None) => return Err(DomainError::SchemaBundleUnknown(bundle_id.to_string()).to_status()),
    95	        Err(e) => return Err(e.to_status()),
    96	    };
    97	
    98	    // Phase 5 GA hardening S8: producer signature verification (per
    99	    // Trace §13). Strict mode requires a verifier and rejects /
   100	    // quarantines events that fail. Non-strict mode still records
   101	    // outcomes via metrics so operators can prepare to flip the flag.
   102	    if cfg.strict_signatures && verifier.is_none() {
   103	        return Err(tonic::Status::failed_precondition(
   104	            "strict_signatures=true but no trust store configured; \
   105	             set SPENDGUARD_CANONICAL_INGEST_TRUST_STORE_DIR or flip \
   106	             strict_signatures=false",
   107	        ));
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    // Backpressure check (best_effort_with_backpressure per Trace §10.1).
   111	    let depth = match query::approximate_backpressure_depth(pool).await {
   112	        Ok(d) => d as u64,
   113	        Err(_) => 0, // soft fail
   114	    };
   115	    let backpressure_active = depth > cfg.backpressure_threshold;
   116	
   117	    let mut results = Vec::with_capacity(req.events.len());
   118	    for evt in req.events {
   119	        let res = process_one(
   120	            pool,
   121	            cfg,
   122	            verifier,
   123	            metrics,
   124	            &evt,
   125	            &bundle,
   126	            route,
   127	            backpressure_active,
   128	        )
   129	        .await;
   130	        results.push(res);

   536	fn cloudevent_to_json(evt: &CloudEvent) -> serde_json::Value {
   537	    use base64::Engine as _;
   538	    serde_json::json!({
   539	        "specversion":     evt.specversion,
   540	        "type":            evt.r#type,
   541	        "source":          evt.source,
   542	        "id":              evt.id,
   543	        "time_seconds":    evt.time.as_ref().map(|t| t.seconds).unwrap_or_default(),
   544	        "time_nanos":      evt.time.as_ref().map(|t| t.nanos).unwrap_or_default(),
   545	        "datacontenttype": evt.datacontenttype,
   546	        "data_b64":        base64::engine::general_purpose::STANDARD.encode(&evt.data),
   547	        "tenantid":        evt.tenant_id,
   548	        "runid":           evt.run_id,
   549	        "decisionid":      evt.decision_id,
   550	        "schema_bundle_id": evt.schema_bundle_id,
   551	        "producer_id":     evt.producer_id,
   552	        "producer_sequence": evt.producer_sequence,
   553	        "signing_key_id":  evt.signing_key_id,
   554	        "predicted_a_tokens": evt.predicted_a_tokens,
   555	        "predicted_b_tokens": evt.predicted_b_tokens,
   556	        "predicted_c_tokens": evt.predicted_c_tokens,
   557	        "reserved_strategy": evt.reserved_strategy,
   558	        "prediction_strategy_used": evt.prediction_strategy_used,
   559	        "prediction_policy_used": evt.prediction_policy_used,
   560	        "tokenizer_tier": evt.tokenizer_tier,
   561	        "tokenizer_version_id": evt.tokenizer_version_id,
   562	        "prediction_confidence": evt.prediction_confidence,

   564	        "cold_start_layer_used": evt.cold_start_layer_used,

   566	        "run_predicted_remaining_steps": evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps,
   567	        "run_steps_completed_so_far": evt.run_steps_completed_so_far,

   575	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, Default)]
   576	struct AggregatorMirrors<'a> {
   577	    model: Option<&'a str>,
   578	    agent_id: Option<&'a str>,
   579	    run_id_mirror: Option<Uuid>,
   580	    prompt_class: Option<&'a str>,
   581	    prompt_class_fingerprint: Option<&'a str>,
   582	}
   583	
   584	fn aggregator_mirrors_from_event<'a>(
   585	    evt: &CloudEvent,
   586	    decoded_data: Option<&'a serde_json::Value>,
   587	    run_id: Option<Uuid>,
   588	) -> AggregatorMirrors<'a> {
   589	    if evt.r#type != "spendguard.audit.decision" && evt.r#type != "spendguard.audit.outcome" {
   590	        return AggregatorMirrors::default();
   591	    }
   592	    let Some(data) = decoded_data.and_then(|v| v.as_object()) else {
   593	        return AggregatorMirrors::default();
   594	    };
   595	    let model = json_nonempty_str(data.get("model"))
   596	        .or_else(|| json_nonempty_str(data.get("model_family")));
   597	    AggregatorMirrors {
   598	        model,
   599	        agent_id: json_nonempty_str(data.get("agent_id")),
   600	        run_id_mirror: run_id,
   601	        prompt_class: json_nonempty_str(data.get("prompt_class")),
   602	        prompt_class_fingerprint: json_nonempty_str(data.get("prompt_class_fingerprint")),
   603	    }
   604	}
   605	
   606	fn json_nonempty_str(value: Option<&serde_json::Value>) -> Option<&str> {
   607	    value
   608	        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
   609	        .map(str::trim)
   610	        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())
   611	}
   612	
   613	fn prediction_columns_from_event(evt: &CloudEvent) -> append::PredictionColumns<'_> {
   614	    let is_decision = evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.decision";
   615	    let is_outcome = evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.outcome";
   616	    let projector_unreachable = evt.run_projection_at_decision_atomic == 0
   617	        && evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps == -1
   618	        && evt.run_steps_completed_so_far == 0;
   619	    let projector_absent_default = evt.run_projection_at_decision_atomic == 0
   620	        && evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps == 0
   621	        && evt.run_steps_completed_so_far == 0;
   622	    let no_projector = !is_decision || projector_unreachable || projector_absent_default;
   623	
   624	    append::PredictionColumns {
   625	        predicted_a_tokens: is_decision
   626	            .then(|| nonzero_i64(evt.predicted_a_tokens))
   627	            .flatten(),
   628	        predicted_b_tokens: is_decision
   629	            .then(|| nonzero_i64(evt.predicted_b_tokens))
   630	            .flatten(),
   631	        predicted_c_tokens: is_decision
   632	            .then(|| nonzero_i64(evt.predicted_c_tokens))
   633	            .flatten(),
   634	        reserved_strategy: is_decision
   635	            .then(|| nonempty(&evt.reserved_strategy))
   636	            .flatten(),
   637	        prediction_strategy_used: is_decision
   638	            .then(|| nonempty(&evt.prediction_strategy_used))
   639	            .flatten(),
   640	        prediction_policy_used: is_decision
   641	            .then(|| nonempty(&evt.prediction_policy_used))
   642	            .flatten(),
   643	        tokenizer_tier: is_decision.then(|| nonempty(&evt.tokenizer_tier)).flatten(),
   644	        tokenizer_version_id: is_decision
   645	            .then(|| uuid_nonempty(&evt.tokenizer_version_id))
   646	            .flatten(),
   647	        prediction_confidence: is_decision
   648	            .then(|| nonzero_f32_decimal(evt.prediction_confidence))
   649	            .flatten(),
   650	        prediction_sample_size: is_decision
   651	            .then(|| nonzero_i64(evt.prediction_sample_size))
   652	            .flatten(),
   653	        cold_start_layer_used: is_decision
   654	            .then(|| nonempty(&evt.cold_start_layer_used))
   655	            .flatten(),
   656	        run_projection_at_decision_atomic: if no_projector {
   657	            None
   658	        } else {
   659	            nonzero_i64_decimal(evt.run_projection_at_decision_atomic)
   660	        },
   661	        run_predicted_remaining_steps: if no_projector || evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps == -1 {
   662	            None
   663	        } else {
   664	            Some(evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps)
   665	        },
   666	        run_steps_completed_so_far: if no_projector {
   667	            None
   668	        } else {
   669	            Some(evt.run_steps_completed_so_far)
   670	        },
   671	        actual_input_tokens: outcome_actual_token(
   672	            evt,
   673	            "actual_input_tokens",
   674	            evt.actual_input_tokens,
   675	        ),
   676	        actual_output_tokens: outcome_actual_token(
   677	            evt,
   678	            "actual_output_tokens",
   679	            evt.actual_output_tokens,
   680	        ),
   681	        delta_b_ratio: is_outcome.then(|| nonzero_f32(evt.delta_b_ratio)).flatten(),
   682	        delta_c_ratio: is_outcome.then(|| nonzero_f32(evt.delta_c_ratio)).flatten(),
   683	    }
   684	}
   685	
   686	fn nonempty(value: &str) -> Option<&str> {
   687	    if value.is_empty() { None } else { Some(value) }
   688	}
   689	
   690	fn uuid_nonempty(value: &str) -> Option<Uuid> {
   691	    if value.is_empty() {
   692	        None
   693	    } else {
   694	        Uuid::parse_str(value).ok()
   695	    }
   696	}
   697	
   698	fn nonzero_i64(value: i64) -> Option<i64> {
   699	    if value == 0 { None } else { Some(value) }
   700	}
   701	
   702	fn nonzero_i64_decimal(value: i64) -> Option<BigDecimal> {
   703	    nonzero_i64(value).map(BigDecimal::from)
   704	}
   705	
   706	fn outcome_actual_token(evt: &CloudEvent, key: &str, extension_value: i64) -> Option<i64> {
   707	    if evt.r#type != "spendguard.audit.outcome" {
   708	        return None;
   709	    }
   710	    if let Ok(serde_json::Value::Object(data)) =
   711	        serde_json::from_slice::<serde_json::Value>(&evt.data)
   712	    {
   713	        if let Some(value) = data.get(key).and_then(json_i64) {
   714	            return (value >= 0).then_some(value);
   715	        }
   716	    }
   717	    (extension_value > 0).then_some(extension_value)
   718	}
   719	
   720	fn json_i64(value: &serde_json::Value) -> Option<i64> {
   721	    value
   722	        .as_i64()
   723	        .or_else(|| value.as_str().and_then(|s| s.parse::<i64>().ok()))
   724	}
   725	
   726	fn nonzero_f32(value: f32) -> Option<f32> {
   727	    if value == 0.0 { None } else { Some(value) }
   728	}
   729	
   730	fn nonzero_f32_decimal(value: f32) -> Option<BigDecimal> {
   731	    nonzero_f32(value).and_then(|v| BigDecimal::from_str(&format!("{v:.3}")).ok())
   732	}

     1	-- ============================================================================
     2	-- 0018_canonical_events_aggregator_mirror_columns.sql
     3	--
     4	-- SLICE_06 R2 B4 (Option A): add first-class mirror columns on
     5	-- canonical_events so the stats_aggregator hot path can group by
     6	-- model / agent_id / run_id / prompt_class / prompt_class_fingerprint
     7	-- with partition-prunable indexes, instead of repeatedly decoding the
     8	-- base64 CloudEvent payload from `payload_json->'data_b64'`.
     9	--
    10	-- Spec ancestors:
    11	--   - docs/stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §4.1 (aggregation source)
    12	--   - docs/audit-chain-prediction-extension-v1alpha1.md §2 (mirror discipline)
    13	--   - docs/slices/SLICE_06_output_predictor_a_b_stats_aggregator.md
    14	--   - 0013_canonical_events_prediction_columns.sql (prior mirror precedent)
    15	--
    16	-- ## R2 review motivation
    17	--
    18	-- R1 panel B4 (DB B1): the SLICE_06 aggregation queries referenced
    19	-- `cloudevent_payload->>'model'` etc., but canonical_events actually
    20	-- carries the CloudEvent envelope at `payload_json` (with the inner
    21	-- data base64-encoded). The queries would raise "column does not exist"
    22	-- at runtime. R2 picks Option A — first-class mirror columns:
    23	--
    24	--   * Faster grouping (no JSON decode + base64 decode per row)
    25	--   * Partition-prunable index covers the canonical hot WHERE shape
    26	--   * Mirror-column write contract follows the same SLICE_01 immutability
    27	--     pattern as the 18 prediction columns in 0013: WRITE-ONCE at INSERT,
    28	--     ALTER COLUMN-ish updates rejected by the existing canonical_events
    29	--     immutability trigger.
    30	--
    31	-- ## Population timeline
    32	--
    33	-- SLICE_06: aggregator queries the new columns; the predictor service
    34	-- does NOT write canonical_events (only canonical_ingest does). Mirror
    35	-- columns are NULL for now because the only producers (sidecar SLICE_10
    36	-- + ledger outbox forwarder) don't yet populate them. Aggregation
    37	-- queries handle NULL by simply skipping rows where the column is NULL
    38	-- — those rows are not yet aggregator-visible. This degrades
    39	-- gracefully: pre-SLICE_10 rows ignored, post-SLICE_10 rows included.
    40	--
    41	-- A tracking GH issue (per R2 plan §"Tracked as GH issues" #14)
    42	-- captures the SLICE_10 producer-side population work.
    43	--
    44	-- ## Additivity (no v1alpha2 spec bump)
    45	--
    46	-- Strictly additive: NULLable columns, no new constraints on existing
    47	-- rows, no trigger churn. Migration 0013's
    48	-- `canonical_events_no_update_delete` trigger (added in
    49	-- 0005_immutability_triggers.sql) already locks ALL rows for UPDATE/
    50	-- DELETE — these columns are write-once at INSERT just like the
    51	-- prediction mirror columns.
    52	--
    53	-- ## Stylistic alignment
    54	--
    55	-- - psql autocommit per SLICE_01 R5 (each ALTER + CREATE INDEX commits)
    56	-- - No down migration file per SLICE_03 R2 M3 convention (rollback via
    57	--   ALTER TABLE DROP COLUMN with safety guard on prod)
    58	-- - Comments are verbose because the migration crosses spec boundaries
    59	--   between canonical_ingest and the aggregator service
    60	-- ============================================================================
    61	
    62	-- Step 1: Add five NULLable mirror columns. TEXT for model / agent_id
    63	-- / prompt_class / prompt_class_fingerprint because the upstream
    64	-- producers carry them as TEXT in CloudEvent JSON. UUID for run_id
    65	-- because it's structurally a UUID per spec §4.1.
    66	ALTER TABLE canonical_events
    67	    ADD COLUMN model                     TEXT,
    68	    ADD COLUMN agent_id                  TEXT,
    69	    ADD COLUMN run_id_mirror             UUID,
    70	    ADD COLUMN prompt_class              TEXT,
    71	    ADD COLUMN prompt_class_fingerprint  TEXT;
    72	
    73	-- Step 2: Length + enum validation. Same shape as 0013's prediction
    74	-- column CHECKs — NOT VALID (avoid re-scan of existing data) + then
    75	-- VALIDATE so new rows are still rejected at write time.
    76	
    77	ALTER TABLE canonical_events
    78	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_model_length_chk
    79	        CHECK (model IS NULL OR (char_length(model) <= 64 AND char_length(model) > 0))
    80	        NOT VALID,
    81	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_agent_id_length_chk
    82	        CHECK (agent_id IS NULL OR (char_length(agent_id) <= 128 AND char_length(agent_id) > 0))
    83	        NOT VALID,
    84	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prompt_class_enum_chk
    85	        CHECK (prompt_class IS NULL OR prompt_class IN (
    86	            'chat_short', 'chat_long', 'code_gen', 'summarization',
    87	            'rag', 'tool_calling', 'vision'))
    88	        NOT VALID,
    89	    ADD CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prompt_class_fingerprint_length_chk
    90	        CHECK (prompt_class_fingerprint IS NULL
    91	               OR (char_length(prompt_class_fingerprint) BETWEEN 4 AND 256))
    92	        NOT VALID;
    93	
    94	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_model_length_chk;
    95	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_agent_id_length_chk;
    96	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prompt_class_enum_chk;
    97	ALTER TABLE canonical_events VALIDATE CONSTRAINT canonical_events_prompt_class_fingerprint_length_chk;
    98	
    99	-- Step 3: Partition-prunable composite index for the stats_aggregator
   100	-- hot aggregation query shape. Per-bucket UPSERT cycle filters by
   101	-- (tenant_id, event_type='spendguard.audit.outcome', ingest_at window).
   102	-- Group by (model, agent_id, prompt_class). Partition pruning via
   103	-- recorded_month lifts the active partition set.
   104	CREATE INDEX canonical_events_aggregator_bucket_idx
   105	    ON canonical_events (tenant_id, recorded_month, model, agent_id, prompt_class)
   106	    WHERE event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome' AND actual_output_tokens IS NOT NULL;
   107	
   108	-- Step 4: Partition-prunable index for the run_length aggregation
   109	-- query shape (per stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §6 — group by
   110	-- (tenant_id, agent_id, run_id) over decision events).
   111	CREATE INDEX canonical_events_aggregator_run_length_idx
   112	    ON canonical_events (tenant_id, recorded_month, agent_id, run_id_mirror)
   113	    WHERE event_type = 'spendguard.audit.decision' AND run_id_mirror IS NOT NULL;
   114	
   115	-- ============================================================================
   116	-- Column comments — match 0013 verbosity for the same audit-chain
   117	-- maintainability reason.
   118	-- ============================================================================
   119	
   120	COMMENT ON COLUMN canonical_events.model IS
   121	    'Mirror of the producer-supplied model name (e.g. "gpt-4o"). Populated by canonical_ingest write path starting SLICE_10. SLICE_06 R2 B4 — aggregator groups by this column. NULL allowed for legacy rows pre-SLICE_10; aggregation queries treat NULL as "row not yet aggregator-visible".';
   122	COMMENT ON COLUMN canonical_events.agent_id IS
   123	    'Mirror of the producer-supplied agent identifier. Aggregator bucket key. Populated SLICE_10+. NULL allowed for legacy rows.';
   124	COMMENT ON COLUMN canonical_events.run_id_mirror IS
   125	    'UUID mirror of the producer-supplied run_id (column suffix _mirror to disambiguate from canonical_events.run_id which is the audit chain anchor). Used by run_length aggregation (spec §6). NULL allowed for legacy + non-run-scoped events.';
   126	COMMENT ON COLUMN canonical_events.prompt_class IS
   127	    'Classifier label per output-predictor-service-spec-v1alpha1.md §8.1 (7-class enum). Used as the stats_aggregator bucket key — NOT prompt_class_fingerprint (output-predictor spec §8.2 closing paragraph: "Aggregator key uses class itself, not fingerprint"). Populated SLICE_10+.';
   128	COMMENT ON COLUMN canonical_events.prompt_class_fingerprint IS
   129	    'SHA-256-hex string per output-predictor-service-spec-v1alpha1.md §8.2 (canonical: v1:{class}|{model}|{message_count}). Audit identifier for the bucket; not used as aggregator GROUP BY key. Populated SLICE_10+.';
   130	
   131	-- ============================================================================
   132	-- DO-block smoke check: confirm the four CHECKs are VALID + indexes are
   133	-- partition-aware (every child partition gets the local index because
   134	-- the parent is partitioned).
   135	-- ============================================================================
   136	DO $$
   137	BEGIN
   138	    SET LOCAL search_path = pg_catalog, pg_temp;
   139	    PERFORM 1 FROM pg_constraint
   140	        WHERE conname = 'canonical_events_prompt_class_enum_chk'
   141	          AND convalidated = TRUE;
   142	    IF NOT FOUND THEN
   143	        RAISE EXCEPTION 'canonical_events_prompt_class_enum_chk not validated';
   144	    END IF;
   145	    PERFORM 1 FROM pg_indexes
   146	        WHERE schemaname = 'public'
   147	          AND indexname = 'canonical_events_aggregator_bucket_idx';
   148	    IF NOT FOUND THEN
   149	        RAISE EXCEPTION 'canonical_events_aggregator_bucket_idx missing';
   150	    END IF;
   151	END $$;

codex
**Blocker**
- None

**Major**
- `services/stats_aggregator/src/drift_detector.rs:609` - `sink.emit` errors leave no cooldown record, but each retry gets a fresh CloudEvent id at `services/stats_aggregator/src/drift_detector.rs:337`. If canonical_ingest commits the immutable alert and the client then sees a timeout/transport error, the next cycle emits a new event id, so canonical_ingest cannot dedupe it and the audit chain can be spammed with duplicate `prediction_drift_alert` rows.

**Minor**
- None
